# Welcome to ACE Studio | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

At ACE Studio, our mission is to build an AI-driven music workstation for the future of music creation.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/#discover-ace-studio)

Discover ACE Studio


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/whats-new)

**What's New**

Discover brand new features with the latest versions.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library)

![Cover](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F58mFKhvPbSDvINW3O70s%252Fvocal.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0787eb9f-1385-49e5-8707-a9ecb7f07d6e&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3365aa49&sv=2)

**AI Vocal Synth**

Generate vocals with MIDI and lyrics.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library)

![Cover](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FRBvkJr5qjU35zGj2wEgo%252Finstrument.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd15f1210-3b5c-441c-a5c7-6e5517ea5fc6&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e67c349&sv=2)

**AI Instruments**

Generate human-level performances with MIDI.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth)

![Cover](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FMNUjb6usim4s5xMtQe5x%252Fcloning.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71c0f170-a974-44ea-b6e2-7883f81df2a1&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c71747f7&sv=2)

**Voice Cloning**

Clone your AI voice by uploading vocal samples.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/daw-integration/ace-bridge-2)

![Cover](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FDvzdpKYv4B13EIvi8Yzc%252Fbridge.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd1873d6-b55f-4a95-a522-ba4d65aebf38&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4bdc3e12&sv=2)

**ACE Bridge**

Integrate ACE into your DAW with bridge plugin.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/add-a-layer)

# ASIO Problem? | Trouble Shooting | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting#block-17508bffde80808294fee6be5e1270f0)

Exclusivity in ASIO


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Whether ACE Studio or any DAW, playback works perfectly under ASIO mode when it's the only application that output sounds. But things may become unexpected when two applications both want to use an ASIO device at the same time.

Most ASIO drivers can only serve one application at the same time due to the purpose of low latency. That means ACE Studio may fail to initialize ASIO driver and not be able to playback when your DAW has been using it, conversely, your DAW may fail to playback when ACE Studio already launched under ASIO mode.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting#block-17508bffde8080a0b0dfc1ecc60ed8c6)

Solutions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting#block-17508bffde8080938bbec6912ebd3750)

**Use ACE Bridge 2**

ACE Bridge 2 is a VST3 instrument plugin for building an audio bridge between ACE Studio and your DAW. It can be installed together with ACE Studio.

With ACE Bridge 2 connected between ACE Studio and your DAW, ACE Studio's playback will be sent directlly to the track in your DAW where ACE Bridge 2 lies, and no audio device will be used by ACE Studio until ACE Bridge 2 is off. In this case, you can hear all sounds come from your DAW with any configured ASIO device.

Please note:If you launch ACE Studio first and select an ASIO device for its audio device before launching your DAW, your DAW may still have problem with playback even the ACE Bridge 2 is on. In this case, you could change the audio device into None in ACE Studio before launching your DAW.

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting#block-17508bffde80800faed1ef9eb838733a)

**Try ASIO4ALL**

ASIO4ALL is an universal ASIO driver, which utilizes low-level WDM drivers to achieve low-latency while keeping a wide compatibility device range. It implements a multi-client ASIO device, a.k.a ASIO4ALL can be used simultaneously by different DAWs.

For how to install and use ASIO4ALL, and more general information on it, please consult their official website: [https://asio4all.org/](https://asio4all.org/)

Please note:ASIO4ALL in general can bring you a low-latency experience, but it may have less-capable performance or a tighter feature set compared to the native ASIO driver provided by your sound card vendor. If ASIO4ALL is not suitable for your case, use ACE Bridge will always be a viable solution.

[NextCan’t launch ACE Studio?](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-studio-issues/cant-launch-ace-studio)

Last updated 3 months ago

---

# Can’t find ACE Bridge plugin in your DAW? | Trouble Shooting | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/cant-find-ace-bridge-plugin-in-your-daw#block-17508bffde80809a9073e8b24a239316)

Wrong list?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ACE Bridge 2 is a VST3/AU/AAX **instrument** plugin.

After installation, you should find it on the VST3/AU/AAX plugin list.

It is an **instrument** plugin, you can insert it on a MIDI track but not an audio track in your DAW.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/cant-find-ace-bridge-plugin-in-your-daw#block-88b1b57e681f444fa71dfaa2f430e115)

Try to rescan


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you are on the right plugin list, but still can not find the bridge plugin. Try to rescan plugins from your DAW plugin management window.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/cant-find-ace-bridge-plugin-in-your-daw#block-17508bffde8080f7bda0d6f61a641a61)

Try to reinstall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you still can’t find the bridge plugin after rescan, try to reinstall ACE Bridge 2.

*   For Win - Reinstall ACE Studio, the bridge will be reinstalled together.
    
*   For Mac - Reinstall ACE Bridge 2 in the preferences window of ACE Studio.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/cant-find-ace-bridge-plugin-in-your-daw#block-17508bffde8080d191aef9ba33269e46)

For Win users


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Try to update your Visual C ++ version with the Microsoft official tool:

*   [https://aka.ms/vs/17/release/vc\_redist.x64.exe](https://aka.ms/vs/17/release/vc_redist.x64.exe)
    

For more details about the VC\_Redist, please refer to [MahmoudGSaleh Latest supported Visual C++ Redistributable downloads](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/cpp/windows/latest-supported-vc-redist?view=msvc-170)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/cant-find-ace-bridge-plugin-in-your-daw#block-17508bffde8080e78a67ead5a28b408a)

Ask for help


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have tried all these methods, but still can’t find ACE Bridge in your DAW. Please contact [\[email protected\]](https://docs.acestudio.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
, we would love to help.

[PreviousCan’t launch ACE Studio?](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-studio-issues/cant-launch-ace-studio)
[NextACE Bridge 2: Special settings in DAW](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-2-special-settings-in-daw)

Last updated 3 months ago

---

# ACE Bridge 2: Special settings in DAW | Trouble Shooting | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-2-special-settings-in-daw#block-18408bffde808042aa7adb4245355949)

Studio One (Windows)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![image](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.spr.so%2Fcdn-cgi%2Fimagedelivery%2Fj42No7y-dcokJuNgXeA0ig%2F989ef341-31c9-4125-8695-5a88c75d6f31%2Fimage%2Fw%3D828%2Cquality%3D90%2Cfit%3Dscale-down&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f3a3b951&sv=2)

Please uncheck this checkbox in the \[Audio Setup\] preferences of Studio One (Only for Windows) to make sure you can start playback independently in ACE Studio when connected to the ACE Bridge 2.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-2-special-settings-in-daw#block-18408bffde8080a38116f9997ec18e38)

Reaper


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![image](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.spr.so%2Fcdn-cgi%2Fimagedelivery%2Fj42No7y-dcokJuNgXeA0ig%2F83a96abe-fea4-420c-bee8-806bde24b653%2Fimage%2Fw%3D828%2Cquality%3D90%2Cfit%3Dscale-down&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bd8b021e&sv=2)

Please uncheck this checkbox in the \[Audio\] preferences of Reaper to make sure you can start playback independently in ACE Studio when connected to the ACE Bridge 2.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-2-special-settings-in-daw#block-18408bffde8080c3848ed05d94e1fb7d)

Cubase


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![image](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.spr.so%2Fcdn-cgi%2Fimagedelivery%2Fj42No7y-dcokJuNgXeA0ig%2F55b5434a-1c89-4fff-8adb-78d216e0bd95%2Fimage%2Fw%3D828%2Cquality%3D90%2Cfit%3Dscale-down&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf0b693f&sv=2)

Please check this checkbox in the \[VST\] - \[Plug-ins\] preferences of Cubase to make sure you can start playback independently in ACE Studio when connected to the ACE Bridge 2.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-2-special-settings-in-daw#block-18408bffde8080b18344e2100fa68201)

Logic


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![image](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.spr.so%2Fcdn-cgi%2Fimagedelivery%2Fj42No7y-dcokJuNgXeA0ig%2F51ae62fc-de67-4f14-a91a-ced020926558%2Fimage%2Fw%3D1920%2Cquality%3D90%2Cfit%3Dscale-down&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6367693c&sv=2)

ACE Bridge 2 will always sync the tempo and time signature from the playhead in Logic when you start the playback under record or AI vocal mode.

If you find the signature is synced one measure ahead, it is because the playback pre-roll settings of Logic.

To fix this issue, you need to open the \[Settings\] of Logic and locate to the \[Audio\] — \[General\] tab, then deselect the “playback pre-roll” check box.

[PreviousCan’t find ACE Bridge plugin in your DAW?](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/cant-find-ace-bridge-plugin-in-your-daw)
[NextACE Bridge Can’t Connect](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-cant-connect)

Last updated 3 months ago

# ACE Bridge Can’t Connect | Trouble Shooting | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-cant-connect#check-for-updates-of-ace-studio)

**Check for updates of ACE Studio**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Open ACE Studio

2

Open preferences window from the main menu

3

Select “Update” tab and click on the “**Update**” button

4

You can also download the latest version from [https://acestudio.ai/download](https://acestudio.ai/download)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-cant-connect#use-ace-bridge-2-instead-of-ace-bridge-1)

**Use ACE Bridge 2 instead of ACE Bridge 1**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Since version 1.9.7 of ACE Studio, the ACE Bridge 1 is no longer supported, please use ACE Bridge 2 instead.

*   For Windows users: The Bridge 2 plugin should be installed automatically with the installation of ACE Studio.
    
*   For Mac users: You can manually install the bridge 2 plugin from the preferences window of ACE Studio.
    

To learn more about the ACE Bridge 2 plugin, please refer to [ACE Bridge 2](https://docs.acestudio.ai/daw-integration/ace-bridge-2)
.

If you encounter any issues with ACE Bridge 2 plugin, please contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.acestudio.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

[PreviousACE Bridge 2: Special settings in DAW](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-2-special-settings-in-daw)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Can’t launch ACE Studio? | Trouble Shooting | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-studio-issues/cant-launch-ace-studio#block-1af08bffde80803cac7df39212a0ed55)

Stuck on the program startup screen


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you got stuck on the program startup screen like the following picture, there are a few things that tend to fix it.

1.  **Restart your device:** This will clear any bad states.
    
2.  **Check for updates of ACE Studio**
    
    *   Open ACE Studio - Open preferences window from the main menu - Select “Update” tab and click on the Update button.
        
    *   You can also download the latest version from [https://acestudio.ai/download](https://acestudio.ai/download)

# Installation | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/installation#install-ace-studio)

Install ACE Studio


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ACE Studio is a desktop application for Windows and macOS. To install ACE Studio, please follow the steps below.

1

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/installation#undefined)

[Download the Installer](https://acestudio.ai/download/)

Click to open the download page.

If you are a Mac user, click the For Mac button to download the installer for macOS.

If you are a Win user, click the For Win button to download the installer for Windows.

2

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/installation#install-with-one-click)

Install with One Click

After the download finishes, open the installer (from your browser's downloads list or your Downloads folder).

The installer runs automatically, installs ACE Studio, and launches it when installation completes.

If installation fails or ACE Studio does not launch, please refer to [Can’t launch ACE Studio?](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-studio-issues/cant-launch-ace-studio)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/installation#system-requirements)

System Requirements

Minimum system version requirements:

*   Windows 10 64-bit Bulid 1809 or later
    
*   macOS 11.0 (Big Sur) or later
    

ACE Studio requires an Internet connection to run.

With cloud rendering, computers with standard configurations can easily run ACE Studio. Meanwhile, we also offer the Turbo Mode feature, which fully utilizes the computing power of your computer to significantly boost AI rendering speed on high-performance machines. For more details, please refer to [Local Rendering](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/installation#reinstall-ace-studio)

Reinstall ACE Studio


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You don't need to uninstall before reinstalling. Simply download and open the latest installer [here](https://acestudio.ai/download/)
, it automatically updates or reinstalls ACE Studio to the newest version.

[PreviousWhat's New](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/whats-new)
[NextTour the Interface](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/tour-the-interface)

# Road Map | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/road-map#upcoming-features)

Upcoming Features


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   New voices including kids voices, country voices, opera voices, rap voices
    
*   New singing languages including French, Portuguese, Italian
    
*   New instruments including saxophones, violins, violas, cellos and winds
    
*   Articulation and expression controls for instruments
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/road-map#planned-features)

Planned Features


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Text to sample: generate sample loops on canvas with the existing content as context
    
*   Text to music: generate a song track with prompt on canvas
    
*   Upgrade for pitch editing tools
    
*   Universal audio to MIDI: convert vocal or instrument sound to MIDI
    
*   ACE ARA plugin: generate and edit AI vocals and AI instruments with MIDIs converted from audio tracks within your DAW.
    
*   Upgrade for ACE Bridge plugin: multi-track support
    
*   AI orchestra: native ensemble strings by sections
    
*   Build-in AI agent: the AI co-producer that can help you work easier and faster in ACE Studio

# Tour the Interface | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

TitleBar and Transport


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FAt3WfZ5Cb0veTGkR7X5F%252FTitleBar%2520nd%2520Transport.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D998aef1c-f96b-4913-bdeb-b390d06a9339&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1fedf319&sv=2)

TitleBar and Transport are located at the top of ACE Studio, displaying core functions such as project name, tempo, time signature, and playback controls.

[Transport](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/tour-the-interface#canvas)

Canvas


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FSoVcQDfUm40IKsYUV9ZK%252FCanvas.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7bfdfc3f-8234-4fc0-b5c5-9f59e72cf457&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e7bb3b6&sv=2)

Canvas is the core area for your music creation, displaying all tracks and clips in the project in a timeline format. Here, you can create, move, trim, and arrange different clips to build a complete song structure.

[Arrangement in Canvas](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/tour-the-interface#clip-editor)

Clip Editor


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F5PehvJ12IkpbM6i4bKzM%252FClip%2520Editor.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29669713-64cb-4a20-ac55-10f7feeb5b7f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ceaf31c3&sv=2)

The Clip Editor is the place for fine-tuning. When you double-click a clip, it expands below. You can edit notes, lyrics, and vocal controls in the Piano Roll, or adjust audio files in the Audio Editor.

[Clip Editor](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips/clip-editor)

Mixer

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FsXlbI36W1pg8ZIA2TVQi%252FMixer.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb8c2b36-1cbc-4dd8-a020-b193d4755829&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=adc081ab&sv=2)

In the Mixer, by adjusting the faders and knobs of each track, you can easily balance the relationships between parts and shape the final mix.

[Mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)

Additional Tracks


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fh7NK77DUH4538VlShBlW%252FAdditional%2520Tracks.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c93b3e7-92b3-4d46-8c72-de78de65d6b1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9897ddca&sv=2)

Additional tracks can be expanded above the Canvas to manage the project's global information and markers. This includes the Time Signature track, Tempo track, and Chord track, making it convenient for you to arrange complex rhythms.

Fx Panel


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FC4Fgoa08dD9iwGr8WXiS%252FFX%2520panel.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48c811fe-93f8-495c-92a0-3eabb5679984&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ed870a05&sv=2)

The effects panel is where you add "seasoning" to the sound. Here, you can load and adjust effect plugins for each track. By using effects such as reverb, equalizer, compression, or AI Choir room effects, you can change and enhance the tonal quality of the tracks.

[Effects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/tour-the-interface#main-menu)

Main Menu


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F7h9SQu4upQ9t3x799iVt%252FPreferences.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1df00a0b-1a30-48ce-9ca5-913c9cc89c5b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a05e841b&sv=2)

The main menu is located in the upper left corner of the ACE Studio interface. Here, you can find all commands such as file management, editing operations, and settings options.

# Vocal Synth Models | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library/vocal-synth-models#model-generation-evolution)

Model Generation Evolution


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ACE Studio continuously iterates its vocal synthesis models. Building on state-of-the-art AI architectures, we incorporate proprietary innovations to enhance naturalness, expressiveness, multilingual accuracy, and voice cloning fidelity.

We also responsibly expand our vocal datasets to cover more languages and musical styles. When architectural improvements and new training data meet our release criteria, we publish a new model generation.

![Select Vocal Synth Models in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FEBy73fsiyTV8fJrPnR3x%252Fmodel_list.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc51015f5-12fa-4841-83b5-082059fdc2a4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=41bf20b9&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library/vocal-synth-models#model-list)

Model List


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Below is the current lineup of model generations and variants:

# Voice Library | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

AI Voices are the sound sources of AI vocals. They generate vocals from MIDI notes and lyrics. You can further shape the performance by editing notes, lyrics, phonemes, pitch, and vocal control parameters.

![The ACE Studio Voice Library window, showing a grid of available AI Voices.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FR8YDSdYs31ix0b3wYbEy%252Fvoice_library.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15a06c21-9af1-4350-aff7-255f992bb641&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=df57041c&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#access-ai-voices)

Access AI voices


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There a 3 ways to browse AI voices from the voice library:

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#browse-from-the-toolbar)

Browse from the Toolbar

![Accessing the ACE Studio Voice Library by clicking from the main toolbar.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FuCnuPO6DxKowfK584hUh%252Fbrowse_voice_from_toolbar.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7eca0f19-19d4-4996-9829-5f236f53e12e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d95cb3f&sv=2)

Click the first icon from the Toolbar to open the voice library, where you can browse all AI voices available. Drag a voice onto the canvas to add it, or click on a voice and then click the canvas to place it.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#browse-form-canvas)

Browse form Canvas

![Opening the ACE Studio Voice Library by double-clicking an empty track on the canvas.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FmYCyS0gs3SyPZumLvb8y%252Fbrowse_voice_from_canvas.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df65e9032-8418-4248-8529-a5ac906dfb2e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d60ba923&sv=2)

Double-click an empty track area on the Canvas to open the Voice Library, where you can browse all AI voices available. Then select a voice to add.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#browse-from-vocal-track-panel)

Browse from Vocal Track Panel

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fiwrnptxi6HfFYC7VJHIj%252FClipboard-20251029-091531-781.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46d5044d-3581-4bd6-962e-172e76f8d7e3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f9235cdf&sv=2)

Click on the picture of vocal track panel to open the Voice Library, where you can browse all AI voices available. You can click to replace the current AI voice. You can also click the "+" in the [AI Choir](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)
 to access the Voice Library and click to add a voice to the choir.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#adding-an-ai-voice-on-canvas)

Adding an AI Voice on Canvas

When you add a voice, it is loaded onto the selected or target track on canvas, and a vocal clip will be created at the corresponding position on the canvas.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#voice-library)

Voice Library


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 5 tabs in the voice library, organizing different sources of voices:

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#pre-made-voices)

Pre-made Voices

Pre-made voices are trained by ACE Studiousing responsibly sourced datasets of professional singers, which highly represents the characters and performances of the singers. We are continuously adding new pre-made voices to meet diverse vocal production needs.

Most of the pre-made voices are royalty-free, you can use them in any commercial production. You can easily generate a license to a royalty-free voice within ACE Studio. For more details, please refer to [Licenses](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/licenses)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#cloned-voices)

Cloned Voices

Your cloned voices are shown under this tab. You can access to the manage page from the voice card. To learn more about cloning your voice, please refer to [Cloning A Voice for Vocal Synth](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth)
.

Cloned voices privately shared with you are also under this tab. For more details, please refer to [Private Share](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/private-share)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#community-voices)

Community Voices

Voices form the community are shown under this tab. These voices are cloned and published by the community of ACE Studio users.

To use a community voice, you need to **collect** it first before adding it to your project.

To learn more about publishing a cloned voice, please refer to [Publishing Cloned Voice](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/publishing-cloned-voice)
.

If the owner of a community voice choose to take the voice down, you will no longer have access to this voice after a 30-day period.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#blended-voices)

Blended Voices

Your saved blended voices are shown under this tab. These voices are stored under your account, you can access them by logging into ACE Studio with your account on any devices.

Right click on the voice card to manage it. You can modify its name, tags, native language, image, or delete it from your account.

To learn more about the feature of blending voices, please refer to [Voice Blending](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/voice-blending)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#choirs)

Choirs

Pre-made choirs and your saved choir presets are shown under this tab.

Right click on your saved choir card to manage it. You can modify its name, tags, native language, or delete it from your account.

To learn more about the feature of AI Choir, please refer to [AI Choir](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#search-for-voices)

Search for Voices

Click on the search bar to activate the search mode. Each AI voice is annotated with a name, native language, and several tags. You can search with text or use the filters to locate a voice you want.

Click on the close button from the right side of the search bar to exit the search mode.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library#filter-for-vocal-synth-models)

Filter for Vocal Synth Models

The filter for vocal synth models is located at the right upper corner of the voice library. You can use it to filter AI voices from a specific vocal synth model.

The same AI voice can be included in multiple generations of vocal synth models, but due to differences between vocal synth models, the AI voice's performance may vary across different models. For more details, please refer to [Vocal Synth Models](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library/vocal-synth-models)
.

With the default option of "All Models", all AI voices are shown in the library with their recommend vocal synth model.

[PreviousRoad Map](https://docs.acestudio.ai/getting-started/road-map)
[NextVocal Synth Models](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library/vocal-synth-models)

Last updated 14 days ago

# Editing Pitch | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#ai-pitch-user-pitch)

AI Pitch/User Pitch


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 2 types of pitch curve in ACE Studio:

*   AI Pitch: AI will generate the pitch based on the current notes, lyrics, and the AI voice. AI pitch displayed as a dark curve under pitch editing mode.
    
*   User Pitch: The user-edited pitch curve will override the AI pitch. User pitch displayed as a white curve under pitch editing mode.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#pitch-tools)

Pitch Tools


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 6 pitch tools to draw, fix, erase, fine-tune pitch curves:

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FqGjprpSry41ILqrbxlJ2%252Fpitch_tool.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D241e8d6a-9c8c-4dd8-a548-8ab4879fd8ef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e08bf077&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#pitch-brush)

Pitch Brush

Pitch brush is the basic tool for rewriting the pitch curve. (shortcut key 1 )

When you select this tool, the piano roll will turn into the pitch editing mode, where you can see AI pitch as dark curve and user pitch as white curve.

With this tool, you can simply draw user pitch curves.

*   Use left click to draw user pitch.
    
*   Use right click to erase user pitch.
    

Tip: You can use a graphics tablet to draw more precise pitch curves.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#pitch-anchor)

Pitch Anchor

Pitch anchor is a more mouse-friendly tool for drawing pitch curves.

Click on the pitch brush to open the drop down, where you can switch to the pitch anchor tool.

Double click to place the first anchor, then click to add the following anchors, right click to end this curve.

You can drag a selection box to select anchors, and move or delete them.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#fixed-brush)

Fixed Brush

Fixed brush is a tool can lock certain parts of the AI pitch as user pitch. (shortcut key 2 )

AI pitch is generated based on the AI voice, melody, and lyrics. Any changes to these elements will result in the regeneration of AI pitch. AI generates AI pitch piece by piece, even you just change one lyric in a piece, all AI pitch in this piece will be regenerated. Using the fixed brush helps prevent unexpected change to the pitch curve.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#pitch-eraser)

Pitch Eraser

Pitch eraser is a tool that can erase any user pitch, including pitch anchors. (shortcut key 3 )

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#vibrato)

Vibrato

Vibrato is a tool that can add a vibrato on a note. (shortcut key 4 )

To create a vibrato, just simply drag on a note from right to left. Before releasing your mouse, drag horizontally to adjust the length, drag vertically to adjust the amplitude (how big the vibrato is).

After releasing, you can see the handles of all parameters:

*   Amplitude - drag the square at the top left corner vertically to modify
    
*   Phase - drag the handle at the left bottom corner horizontally to modify
    
*   Frequency - drag the handle at the right bottom corner horizontally to modify
    
*   Envelopes (attack and release) - drag the to circles in the middle to control the envelopes
    

Under this tool, you can drag a selection box to select one to more vibratos, then you can delete them.

Tip: Usually, for a longer note, the AI pitch already has a vibrato. In this case, if you add an extra vibrato on it, the final pitch would be in chaos. You can draw a flat user pitch first, then add a vibrato on it to make the result more natural.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#modulation)

Modulation

Modulation is a tool that can control the dynamic range of pitch curve. (shortcut key 5 )

Drag on a note vertically to control the dynamic.

*   Drag down to make the pitch more flat
    
*   Drag up for the opposite
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch#unvoiced-pitch)

Unvoiced Pitch


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Dash pitch curve is voiceless pitch, this means the sound of this part is voiceless (breathy voice or aspirated sound).

When you are drawing pitch curve on voiceless consonants or blank area without any AI pitch, you will draw voiceless pitch by default.

*   To draw voiceless pitch, hold Alt / ⌥ Option while drawing.
    
*   To force drawing voice pitch anywhere, hold Shift + Alt / ⌥ Option while drawing.
    

[PreviousEditng Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics)
[NextVocal Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Vocal Controls | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Vocal Controls are a new set of advanced parameters designed for vocal synth models of Verse25 and later, allowing for fine-tuned control over the AI singer's performance. These parameters replace most of the previous emotion controls.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#what-are-vocal-controls)

What Are Vocal Controls


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Vocal Controls allow users to fine-tune the vocal performance of AI singers by adjusting specific vocal qualities such as Power, Soft, Breathy, and Chest. These controls are designed to give users precise control over how the AI singer sounds, making the performance more expressive and tailored to the song's needs.

![An overview of the Vocal Controls parameter lanes in ACE Studio, including Power, Soft, Breathy and Chest.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FI1ZL9iGXpMM4AcsPjQ69%252Fvocal_controls.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc47a6802-06fc-40b1-8ec8-bfbb44f21437&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65efaa3f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#basic-controls)

Basic Controls

Basic Controls consist of four adjustable parameters available to all AI singers.

Power[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#power)

“Power” controls the strength and intensity of the vocal delivery. Increasing this parameter gives the voice more energy and impact, ideal for powerful choruses or dramatic moments.

Soft[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#soft)

“Soft” adjusts the overall gentleness and smoothness of the voice. Higher softness makes the voice sound more delicate and soothing, suitable for ballads or intimate moments.

Breathy[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#breathy)

“Breathy” controls the amount of airiness or breath-like quality in the voice. Increasing this parameter adds a whispery, ethereal texture, perfect for dreamy or emotional passages.

Chest[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#chest)

“Chest” enhances the resonance and depth in the lower vocal range, giving the voice a fuller and more grounded tone. This is useful for creating a warm and rich vocal presence.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#special-controls)

Special Controls

Special Controls can be configured exclusively within specific singers that support these features.

Rap[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#rap)

"Rap" controls the rap style of the voice. Increasing this parameter enhances the clarity, speed, and rhythm of the articulation, making the voice more aggressive and street-like. It is suitable for rap sections in hip-hop music, pop songs, or any passages requiring strong rhythmic expression.

Opera[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#opera)

"Opera" injects classical bel canto singing techniques into the voice. Increasing this parameter enhances the resonance and penetration of the voice, adds brilliant vibrato and dramatic tone, making the voice sound more bright and full. It is ideal for singing classical arias, brilliant segments in musicals, or adding a grand, epic feeling to songs.

Chinese Opera[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#chinese-opera)

"Chinese Opera" adds the unique charm and singing style of traditional Chinese opera to the voice. Increasing this parameter makes the articulation more distinctive, the tone brighter and higher-pitched, and incorporates the common melismatic and ornamental sounds of Chinese opera. It is suitable for singing opera excerpts or integrating "Chinese style" elements into modern music.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#auto)

Auto

When no manual edits are made, the AI automatically infers and generates the performance based on the context of melody, lyrics, and the current AI voice's singing style.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#editing-vocal-controls)

Editing Vocal Controls


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Drawing a curve for a Vocal Control parameter in ACE Studio by clicking and dragging.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F7bf5OKD5SAvxWFHtvvyS%252Fedit_vocal_controls.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a447301-f2e6-4513-a568-ecd5c2081570&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98ce527f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#editing-parameter-envelope)

Editing Parameter Envelope

To create or modify a parameter envelope, simply **left-click and drag** within the parameter lane.

To remove your parameter evelope, **right-click and drag** over the envelope. The erased area will return to "Auto" mode.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls#global-control)

Global Control

Located to the left of the parameter track, the Global Control Knob allows you to apply a consistent offset. The final value you see and hear is a combination of your manual drawing and the global knob's setting.

When a parameter lane is completely in Auto Mode, you can still adjust it, but it will only take effect once you draw an envelope.

[PreviousEditing Pitch](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch)
[NextEmotion Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Breath | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

![Add breath and adjusting the duration of a breath in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fe00VctWZSBdgJnOsLJTh%252Fbreath.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5101a370-b008-4911-8a97-14e829086b1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab526e0f&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath#what-is-breath)

What is Breath


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Just like human singers, adding a breath at the beginning of a sentence usually makes the vocal performance sound more natural. This is especially helpful for long sentences or high notes, where breaths provide a sense of realism and emotional connection.

Breath is the first tab in the AI parameters panel, allowing users to add breaths to the beginning of vocal lines for enhanced realism and expressiveness.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath#editing-breath)

Editing Breath


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath#adding-breath)

Adding Breath

Automatic Addition

Manual Addition

Click on the Add all button from the left panel to automatically add breaths to the entire clip. It will intelligently place breaths at appropriate positions.

Click on the dark purple area to manually add a breath.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath#adjusting-breath-duration)

Adjusting Breath Duration

You can adjust the duration of a breath by dragging the left edge of the breath note.

[PreviousEmotion Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls)
[NextSinging Languages](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/singing-languages)

# Use Cases | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

This chapter will demonstrate through a series of real application scenarios how to use the core functions of ACE Studio to tackle specific creative challenges, simplify complex workflows, and inspire new musical ideas.

[Edit Vocal from a Mixed Track](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/edit-vocal-from-a-mixed-track)
[Choir Rehearsal](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/choir-rehearsal)
[Song Writing](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/song-writing)

# How to Fine-tune the Pitch Curve | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-fine-tune-the-pitch-curve#aggressive-pitch)

Aggressive pitch


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252Fm5bHtWenjrU7fjhsTgBl%252FAggressive%2520pitch.avif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f92f5be-591c-409f-9952-9e77b382d078&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7f889&sv=2)

Draw an overshot at the beginning of the note to make it sound more aggressive.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-fine-tune-the-pitch-curve#sigh-at-the-end)

Sigh at the end


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252FSNjkTV5HIAgxYLcDv8jd%252FSigh%2520at%2520the%2520end.avif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0deccab2-6d8a-4ba5-b6ce-3adcc4402532&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1e4cdae&sv=2)

Draw an overshot at the end of a long note to create a sigh.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-fine-tune-the-pitch-curve#short-peak-in-the-middle)

Short peak in the middle


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252F5865nPD9ZljSsrqxPBJD%252FShort%2520peak%2520in%2520the%2520middle.avif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d935fee-e958-428a-bf86-bd78f702f7fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=851478aa&sv=2)

This type of pitch can create Viking, Mongolian, and other ethnic singing styles for cinematic vocals.

# Editng Lyrics | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Enter lyrics for your melody to generate an AI vocal. The lyric system follows these rules:

*   If a note has no lyric, ACE Studio uses a default lyrics.
    
*   Each note corresponds to one syllable only.
    
*   You can use a "-" (dash) to indicate a melismatic note, allowing the previous syllable to extend across multiple notes without adding a new syllable.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#edit-lyrics)

Edit Lyrics


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 3 ways to edit lyrics:

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#edit-line-by-line)

Edit line by line

![Typing lyrics line-by-line below in ACE Studio piano roll.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fvqf4b1WyYHFp6UGFafbn%252Fedit_line_by_line.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1cba841-1c02-4d8a-99fa-531d8313f8e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9f5bc1d7&sv=2)

Click on the text line below notes to type in lyrics line by line.

*   Press Enter or click outside of the text box to apply these lyrics.
    
*   By applying these lyrics, they will be split into syllables and those syllables will be filled into syllabic notes one by one.
    
    *   If the number of syllables is larger than syllabic notes, the extra syllables will take place on existing melismatic notes until all melismatic notes are used, then the rest syllables will be discarded.
        
    *   "\_" (underscore) shows an empty lyric.
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#edit-on-a-note)

Edit on a note

![Editing a lyric by double-clicking a single note within the ACE Studio piano roll.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FlUZqRIgZJovoiOobKwN2%252Fedit_on_note.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da9ea9f14-d773-47d2-bae3-49077c1a4b90&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a3331b50&sv=2)

Double-click a note to enter lyrics. ACE Studio splits the text into syllables and assigns them to the current note and the following notes in order.

*   Press Enter or click outside the text box to apply the lyrics.
    
*   By applying these lyrics, all content you type in will replace the original lyrics on notes, including "-"(dash).
    
*   Press Tab to move to the next note.
    
*   If a syllable is unsupported or unrecognized in the selected language, that note is synthesized with the default syllable (e.g., “da”).
    

This method is for correcting the lyrics of individual notes. We recommend using the line-by-line method to edit the entire lyrics.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#edit-with-lyrics-panel)

Edit with lyrics panel

![Edit lyrics with lyrics panel in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FPvg19zN3oMOg2JxWpqly%252Fedit_lyric_panel.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc47475d1-9dfc-4dae-9f13-fd7d95ee5667&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff39ba77&sv=2)

To edit lyrics with full vision, you can use the lyrics panel.

Select multiple notes, and select “Edit lyrics” from the right-click menu to open the lyrics panel.

> **Keyboard Shortcuts:**
> 
> macOS: ⌘ Command + E
> 
> Windows: Ctrl + E

*   In the lyrics panel, it shows all lyrics from selected notes.
    
*   **Skip Tenuto**: By checking this box, it will skip all melismatic notes when filling syllables into notes.
    
*   **Fill the Rest Lyrics**: By checking this box, if there are remaining syllables after filling the selected notes with lyrics, those syllables will continue to be assigned to the subsequent notes. Otherwise, they will be discarded.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#note-languages)

Note Languages

Each note has its own language attribute. When a lyric of another language being filled into a note, the language of this note will switch to the new one.

If lyrics with a mismatched language are entered on the note, a red warning indicator will appear above the note.

To learn more details about languages, please refer to [Singing Languages](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/singing-languages)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#edit-phonemes-and-consonants)

Edit Phonemes and Consonants


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every syllable is built around a single vowel and can include consonants. Since each note represents one syllable, it also contains one vowel and its associated consonants.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#edit-phonemes)

Edit Phonemes

Phonemes are the most basic pronunciation information in vocal synthesis. Phonemes are automatically recognized based on the lyrics and displayed above each note. Generally, you don't need to edit them manually. You can also double-click to edit them.

If you want to manually edit phonemes, you can refer to the standard phoneme dictionary for each language in [Phoneme Dictionary](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/phoneme-dictionary)
.

Tip: "cl" represents a voiceless sound or a glottal stop used in Japanese to indicate a brief pause or rhythmic separation in speech or singing.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#pre-post-consonants)

Pre/Post Consonants

This feature is only supported by vocal synth models of Verse24 and earlier.

Consonants are darker box at both side of a note.

*   A pre consonant is positioned before the note, just outside the left boundary of the note.
    
*   A post consonant is positioned at the end of the note, but within the right boundary of the note.
    

The duration of consonant pronunciation is often an important factor influencing accents.

*   AI will generate the duration for each consonant based on the accent of AI voice being used on track.
    
*   To adjust the duration of a consonant, just simply drag on its left boundary.
    

The durations of consonants will be fixed once they have been generated by AI, unless you change them manually or change the lyrics. For example, you have a MIDI clip with lyrics on notes, and you let AI generate the vocal by starting the playback. At this moment, the durations of consonants are fixed and you can see the darker boxes around notes. These durations come from the accent of the current AI voice on the track, if you want to change the AI voice, you can clear all the durations of consonants by selecting all notes and click “Clear all consonants” from the right-click menu.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#voiceless-consonants)

Voiceless Consonants

This feature is only supported by vocal synth models of Verse24 and earlier.

Consonants like “s, t, k, p, b, etc.” are voiceless consonants. They produce sound through the airflow in mouth rather than through the vocal cords, so usually they don’t have pitch.

[PreviousEditing Notes](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes)
[NextEditing Pitch](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Add a Breath | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Just like human singers, adding a breath at the beginning of a sentence usually brings much natural result, especially for a long sentence or high notes.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252FvAEofmLTiV6lqmz87fWU%252Fbreath.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4559d3ef-28e2-45b0-8a47-edd98a11fb73&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2016ea84&sv=2)

The first tab of [Vocal Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls)
 is breath, where you can add a breath at the beginning of each line.

Click on the dark purple area to add a breath.

You can adjust the duration by dragging on the left edge of a breath note.

Learn more: [Breath](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath)

[PreviousAdd Vibrato or Remove AI-generated Vibrato](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/add-vibrato-or-remove-ai-generated-vibrato)

Last updated 2 months ago

 on this track from the canvas with MIDI notes as its content.

FAQ


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Can I import MIDI or MusicXML files?[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds#can-i-import-midi-or-musicxml-files)

Yes. You can import your MIDI or MusicXML files into ACE Studio. For more information, please refer to [Import Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files)
.

Can I control the articulations for specific instruments?[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds#can-i-control-the-articulations-for-specific-instruments)

Yes. You can make the instrument's sound better match your requirements by using [Expression Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/expression-controls)
.

# Edit Vocal from a Mixed Track | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

In ACE Studio, you can edit the vocal from an existing song track with AI tools: [Stem Splitter](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/stem-splitter)
 & [Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics)
.

1

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/edit-vocal-from-a-mixed-track#split-into-stems)

Split into stems

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252FNU1iDB0D4Enczibl6kKT%252Fstemsplitter_split.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0795475e-b54e-430a-806b-771c9aab9ba1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c05cf341&sv=2)

Import your song track into ACE Studio, use the **2 trakcs: Vocal / Instrumental** mode in [Stem Splitter](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/stem-splitter)
, click Split.

Then, you can get a vocal track and an instrumental track down below the original track.

2

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/edit-vocal-from-a-mixed-track#block-17708bffde8080b28256dffae111887c)

Convert vocal to MIDI and lyrics

Drag and drop the vocal clip on a singer track.

In the pop up window, select the right language of the vocal track. If there are more than 1 language in the vocal track, please split the clip to make each clip in one language.

Click the Convert button to start the process.

3

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/edit-vocal-from-a-mixed-track#block-17708bffde808059bf3bc29826e39a45)

Edit your vocal

After the conversion, you have the vocal clip with the recognized lyrics, and an instrumental track.

Now you can start editing on the MIDI clip. (The lyrics recognized from the vocal audio might not be exactly the same, but have at least similar pronunciations.)

[PreviousUse Cases](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases)
[NextChoir Rehearsal](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/choir-rehearsal)

# Add Vibrato or Remove AI-generated Vibrato | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

The AI vocal synth model generates vibrato effects at certain points based on MIDI information and the characteristics of the AI voices, among other factors. However, you might want a different result than the model's default. Let's learn how to manually add vibrato or remove the vibrato generated by AI.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/add-vibrato-or-remove-ai-generated-vibrato#block-19b08bffde8080a0b745ead367a701b4)

Add a vibrato


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Vibrato is more suitable for longer notes, and the pitch of this note is relatively steady.

\[pic\]

To add a vibrato on a note, you can use the vibrato tool from the pitch tool bar in the piano roll. After this vibrato tool selected, drag on a note to create the envelope.

To learn more about using this tool, please refer to

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/add-vibrato-or-remove-ai-generated-vibrato#block-19b08bffde80801baa70faa0d4bf79ba)

Remove/edit AI-generated vibrato


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sometimes, AI will generate the default pitch with vibratos, this is because AI is trying to replicate the singer’s real performance.

\[pic\]

There are 2 methods to remove this kind of vibrato:

1.  Use the pitch brush to draw a steady pitch curve.
    
2.  Use the modulation tool to make pitch flat: on the note you want to modify, long-press the left mouse button and drag down to smooth out the pitch line; if you drag it all the way down, the pitch will become a straight line. The white line in the image below is the pitch smoothed by the Modulation tool, while the gray line is the original pitch generated by the model. To learn more about the modulation tool, please refer to
    

If you still want a vibrato, but need to edit it. You can firstly use the modulation tool to remove the default vibrato, and then use the vibrato tool to add an editable vibrato envelope on the note you want to modify.

[PreviousHow to Create a Children's Choir](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-create-a-childrens-choir)
[NextAdd a Breath](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/add-a-breath)

Last updated 2 months ago

---

# Create AI Instrument sounds in 1 min | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/create-ai-instrument-sounds-in-1-min#create-a-instrument-clip)

Create a Instrument Clip


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the second icon (AI Instruments) in the Tool Bar to open the Instrument Library. Drag and drop a instrument onto the Canvas to create a Instrument Clip. Double-click the Clip to open the piano roll.

You can try different AI voices in the Voice Library. Learn more: [Arrangement in Canvas](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas)
, [Instrument Library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/create-ai-instrument-sounds-in-1-min#input-melodies)

Input Melodies


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, your cursor is on “Note Move” mode, which is to select and move notes, but you can create a half-block note by double-click.

Select the second tool “Note Brush” from the tool bar at top of piano roll, then you can draw notes on the grid by dragging.

You can also input melodies by importing MIDI/MusicXML files. Learn more: [Editing Notes](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes)
, [Import Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/create-ai-instrument-sounds-in-1-min#play-and-export)

Play and Export


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the grid before all notes in piano roll to place the marker-line.

Press Spacebar to start the playback. It will take seconds to render the vocal, when the rendering is done, the playback will continue automatically.

Click the Export button at the top of ACE Studio window.

Choose your preferred format and hit Export to get your audio file.

Learn more: [Export Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files)

This is how easy it is to use AI Instruments in ACE Studio.

[PreviousMake a Vocal in 1 min](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/make-a-vocal-in-1-min)
[NextUse Cases](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases)

# Editing Notes | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#tools-for-notes)

Tools for Notes


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 3 tools that you can play with for MIDI note editing:

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FCq5Z1lMJxnMJMiuFfyoS%252Fnote_tool_vocal.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b08f9bc-aa6a-4a4f-ad64-fc349ca49cdb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d752df28&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#note-mover)

Note Mover

![Using the Note Mover tool in ACE Studio to create and move MIDI notes in the piano roll.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fpk8PLHqAwCKCnVcyZq2i%252Fnote_mover_gif.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b8cffe8-899a-4418-93e3-f647eacc1b22&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d4d2957&sv=2)

Note mover is the default tool for creating, selecting, moving, and resizing notes. (shortcut key V )

*   Double click and drag to create a note with specific length.
    
*   Click on a note to select it. Drag out a selection box to select multiple notes and create a selection, you can also select multiple notes by clicking the first note and the last note while holding Shift . Then you can move, adjust, delete, cut, copy, duplicate them.
    
*   Drag on any note or selected notes to move them.
    
    *   When moving notes, they will snap to grid by default. Hold Ctrl / ⌘ Command to move without snapping.
        
    *   You can also use arrow keys ↑ ↓ ← → to move notes. (hold Shift and use ↑ ↓ to shift by octave)
        
    
*   Drag on the left/right edge of a note to adjust its duration (shortcut key Shift + ← →). It snaps to grid by default, hold Ctrl / ⌘ Command to adjust without snapping.
    
    *   When selecting multiple notes, you can adjust their durations together.
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#note-brush)

Note Brush

![Drawing a series of notes with the Note Brush tool in ACE Studio's piano roll.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FefSuknR1fuG9OKgdfE8Z%252Fnote_brush_gif.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1754fe8-21cf-4d05-bbe1-3461d1119f80&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e9a0547&sv=2)

Note brush is a tool for drawing notes. (shortcut key B )

*   Drag to create a note with specific length. It will snap to grid by default, hold Ctrl / ⌘ Command to move without snapping.
    
*   Draw within the range of a note to create a melismatic note.
    
*   Drag on an existing note to move it.
    
*   Drag on the left/right edge of a note to adjust its duration.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#note-slicer)

Note Slicer

![Splitting a long note into two using the Note Slicer tool in ACE Studio's MIDI editor.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F3QEvGjpXzsLy08vdHepa%252Fnote_slicer_gif.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db893ce6e-b35e-4fe4-8555-0e5d4e363d7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2132c7ab&sv=2)

Note slicer is a tool to create a melismatic note inside a note. (shortcut key X )

*   Click on a note to split. It will snap to grid by default, hold Ctrl / ⌘ Command to dismiss snap.
    

Tip: Adding a short grace note (acciaccatura) at the beginning can enhance the natural flow of the melody.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#grid-and-snap)

Grid and Snap

![A note automatically snapping to the grid in ACE Studio, demonstrating the Grid and Snap feature.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FZQGHzJRqlVOjg6cPnij3%252Fgrid_gif.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80089c0c-ba54-48b9-abdd-fc6b3ca9add1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d896639&sv=2)

Set up Grid and Snap to control how notes align with the grid. This ensures precision when editing melody.

*   Auto-Narrow: Automatically adjusts the grid size to narrow spacing based on the zoom level of the piano roll.
    
*   Auto-Medium (default): Automatically adjusts the grid size to medium spacing based on the zoom level of the piano roll.
    
*   Auto-Wide: Automatically adjusts the grid size to wide spacing based on the zoom level of the piano roll.
    
*   1-16 Cell/Beat: Divides each beat into 1-16 grid cell.
    
*   Snap off: Disables snapping to the grid. Allows free placement of notes and events without alignment to the timeline.
    

Tips: You can input triplets by selecting 3 Cell/Beat.

![Setting the grid to '3 Cell/Beat' in ACE Studio to input triplets.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FCCQCysJ8tQQcnTUdaOOh%252Ftriplets_gif.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa9c611a-c4a5-43a2-b37e-12d0be75f217&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fbe38438&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#monophonic)

Monophonic


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In a vocal track, each vocal clip can only support monophonic content (solo melody).

*   When notes overlap by being moved, the left one will be cut to avoid overlapping.
    
*   When importing a MIDI file, all overlapped notes will be turned into melismatic notes.
    

The length of a note also has a maximum limit. The maximum note length supported by different synthesis models varies, as detailed below:

*   In Verse25, the note length should be less than 20s.
    
*   In Verse24 and earlier, the note length should be less than 18s.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#chords-scale-background)

Chords/Scale Background


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the background switch to turn on/off the chords/scale background.

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#scale)

Scale

*   When the scale background is enabled, tones within the scale will be highlighted.
    
*   Click the expand button on the right side to the settings, where you can switch the background view between scale and chords, set up scales and keys, fold all non-scale tones.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#chords)

Chords

*   When the chords background is enabled, tones within the chords will be highlighted.
    
*   Click the expand button on the right side to the settings, where you can switch the background view between scale and chords, fold all tones out of chords.
    

> To learn about creating a chord progression, please refer to [Chord Track](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track)
> .

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#preview-sound)

Preview Sound


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a piano key in the piano roll is clicked, or when a note is clicked, moved, or created, the corresponding pitch will be played in the piano key sound by default. You can click on the speaker icon on the upper left of the piano keys to turn off the sound.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes#shortcuts)

Shortcuts


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Action

Shortcut Key

Use Note Mover Tool

V

Use Note Brush tool

B

Use Note Slicer tool

X

Move notes

↑ ↓ ← →

Move notes by octave

Shift + ↑ ↓

Adjust note duration

Shift + ← →

Dismiss snap

Hold Ctrl / ⌘ Command

[PreviousCreating AI Vocals](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals)
[NextEditng Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics)
