# Singing Languages | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Each AI singer is multilingual, with specific multilingual support depending on the model version. While each singer has their own **native language** where they perform optimally, this does not mean they are limited to their native language.

Within a clip, you can assign a different language attribute to each note, enabling the AI voice to sing lyrics in various languages on a note-by-note basis.

To ensure optimal performance, it’s important that the lyrics match the language attribute assigned to the note.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/singing-languages#default-singing-language-of-a-track)

Default singing language of a track


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each singer track has its own default singing language setting, which corresponds to the interface language by default. You can set the default language of the track to follow the interface language, the singer's native language, or any specified language in the [preferences window](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences)
.

If you don’t need vocals in other languages, you usually don’t need to change the singing language settings as long as the interface language is the one you need.

The **track default singing language** determines the language of notes created within the track, regardless of their native singing language.

Change it on track header

Change it in piano roll

Right click on the track header, select the target language from the "Default language of notes" drop down.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fckq7QJGPmC9sHnBpbLwV%252Fdefault_language_of_notes.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D138e7368-bec2-4623-a9a2-2a43e6b4002b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90e938d0&sv=2)

When no notes are selected, select the target language from the second drop down in the toolbar of the piano roll.

![Change Singing Languages in ACE Studio piano roll.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fl3j0cHrz0xmjElbEy1lf%252Fsinginglanguages_pianoroll.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65655bc9-2921-4def-bee5-67ae6e532447&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe6ccdeb&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/singing-languages#editing-note-languages)

Editing Note languages


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can change the language of a note by selecting it and choosing the target language from the piano roll's tool bar.

Just remember, the lyrics on these note will not be translated automatically. You need to change the lyrics manually after changing the language attribute.

![Editing note languages in ACE Studio piano roll.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FHVMO8XG0EJdDZfdOdUWO%252Fnote_languages.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31c9bbee-831a-4aa2-8c2e-d319bea9a878&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86645e45&sv=2)

[PreviousBreath](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath)
[NextAI Choir](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Editing Notes | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes#tools-for-notes)

Tools for Notes


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 2 tools that you can play with for instrument MIDI note editing:

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F6xov1DJuh1OGLuNaV0JL%252Fnote_tool_instrument.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3467559-cc39-4405-a314-911938247498&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=93583bb6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes#note-mover)

Note Mover

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F5mA2pI6jExpSz0ML6xzS%252FClipboard-20251029-093612-066.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3049b51-d9e7-4dc2-9c48-070078326be5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cec55f69&sv=2)

Note mover is the default tool for create, selecting, moving, and adjusting notes. (shortcut key V )

*   Double click on grid to create a note with a default length of half a cell. Drag before releasing your mouse to adjust its length.
    
*   Click on a note to select it. Drag out a selection box to select multiple notes and create a selection, you can also select multiple notes by clicking the first note and the last note while holding Shift . Then you can move, adjust, delete, cut, copy, duplicate them.
    
*   Drag on any note or selected notes to move them.
    
    *   When moving notes, they will snap to grid by default. Hold Ctrl / ⌘ Command to move without snapping.
        
    *   You can also use arrow keys ↑ ↓ ← → to move notes. (hold Shift and use ↑ ↓ to move notes by octave)
        
    
*   Drag on the left/right edge of a note to adjust its duration (shortcut key Shift + ← →). It snaps to grid by default, hold Ctrl / ⌘ Command to move without snapping.
    
    *   When selecting multiple notes, you can adjust their durations together.
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes#note-brush)

Note Brush

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FElEBU78GQ7NEm91BYty6%252FClipboard-20251029-093941-443.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e0bdb01-e288-435c-9e80-0af709a9bacc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f30106ce&sv=2)

Note brush is a tool for drawing notes. (shortcut key B )

*   Drag to create a note with specific dimensions. It will snap to grid by default, hold Ctrl / ⌘ Command to move without snapping.
    
*   Draw within the range of a note to create a melismatic note.
    
*   Drag on an existing note to move it.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes#grid-and-snap)

Grid and Snap

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FRdop4V7JgkbS7AgBZDNR%252FClipboard-20251029-094330-995.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9d754c4-70f3-459e-ae99-43ba47f655b0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3cff5a4&sv=2)

The Grid and Snap feature allows you to control how notes align with the timeline. This ensures precision when editing your melody.

*   Auto-Narrow: Automatically adjusts the grid size to narrow spacing based on the zoom level of the piano roll.
    
*   Auto-Medium(default): Automatically adjusts the grid size to medium spacing based on the zoom level of the piano roll.
    
*   Auto-Wide: Automatically adjusts the grid size to wide spacing based on the zoom level of the piano roll.
    
*   1-16 Cell/Beat: Divides each beat into 1-16 grid cell.
    
*   Snap off: Disables snapping to the grid. Allows free placement of notes and events without alignment to the timeline.
    

Tips: You can input triplets by selecting 3 Cell/Beat.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FCCQCysJ8tQQcnTUdaOOh%252Ftriplets_gif.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa9c611a-c4a5-43a2-b37e-12d0be75f217&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fbe38438&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes#chords-scale-background)

Chords/Scale Background


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes#scale)

Scale

*   Click on the scale button to turn on/off the background.
    
*   Click the little triangle at right side to show the settings, where you can set up the scale and fold all notes out of this scale.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes#chord)

Chord

In the settings of background, you can switch to chord mode from the first drop down menu.

With chord background mode, it shows all notes under current chord with color. To learn about creating a chord progression, please refer to [Chord Track](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes#preview-sound)

Preview Sound


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When the piano keyboard is clicked, or when a note is clicked, moved, or created, the default preview sound of the current instrument will play. You can click on the speaker icon on the upper left of the piano keys to turn off the sound.

# Instrument Library | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FteV0fcDiEwBOePqpJbyZ%252Finstrument%2520lib.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd82fe4e9-c2a4-4e6e-a84e-9a74f554a217&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4157a024&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#access-ai-instruments)

Access AI Instruments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There a 3 ways to browse AI instruments from the instrument library:

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#browse-from-the-toolbar)

Browse from the Toolbar

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FwwsVK2eB7QPmlfpLcXlj%252FClipboard-20251029-092355-375.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6933d79c-8018-4a79-889d-64b63b4a89b3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=566c51ab&sv=2)

Click on the second icon from the Toolbar to open the instrument library, where you can browse all AI instruments available. Drag a instrument on the canvas to add to your current project, you can also click on the instrument and click again on the canvas to do so.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#browse-form-canvas)

Browse form Canvas

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F7MgBwZI6HfJBf3visqMR%252FClipboard-20251029-092727-036.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b2bac1c-4ff7-490f-9ce4-181cfb7f85e7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b0b45f0&sv=2)

Double click on any empty tracks from canvas to open the instrument library, where you can browse all AI instruments available. Then you can select a instrument to add to your current project.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#browse-from-instrument-track-panel)

Browse from Instrument Track Panel

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FPOpklCFexydJDjVurlJ9%252FClipboard-20251029-092917-289.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72782a9b-c92b-4391-9a30-a7b47effd5ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b4250a3&sv=2)

Click on the picture of instrument track panel to open the Instrument Library, where you can browse all AI instruments available. You can drag and drop instrument into [Ensembles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#ensembles)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#adding-an-ai-instrument-on-canvas)

Adding an AI Instrument on Canvas

Through the above operations, the corresponding track on the canvas will load this instrument, and a instrument clip will be created at the corresponding position on the canvas.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#instrument-library)

Instrument Library


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 2 tabs in the instrument library:

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#pre-made-instruments)

Pre-made Instruments

Pre-made instruments are crafted by ACE Studio using datasets of professional musicians and their performances in a responsible way. These instruments faithfully capture the unique characteristics and expressive qualities of the original players. We are continuously adding new pre-made instruments to meet diverse music production needs.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#ensembles)

Ensembles

Pre-made ensembles and your saved ensemble presets are shown under this tab.

Right click on your saved enssemble card to manage it. You can modify its name and tags, or delete it from your account.

To learn more about the feature, please refer to [Ensembles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library#search-instruments)

Search Instruments

Click on the search bar to activate the search mode. You can search with text to locate a instrument you want.

Click on the close button from the right side of the search bar to deactivate the search mode.

[PreviousVoice Blending](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/voice-blending)
[NextCreate Instrument Sounds](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds)

# Emotion Controls | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Emotion controls are supported by vocal synth models of Verse24 and earlier. If you are using models of Verse25 and later, please refer to [Vocal Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls)
. To learn more about the differences between various model versions, please refer to [Vocal Synth Models](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library/vocal-synth-models)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#what-are-emotion-parameters)

What Are Emotion Parameters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Emotion parameters will be generated by AI based on the singing style of the current AI voice. You can modify them with envelope or rewrite them directly.

![The Emotion Controls parameters in ACE Studio, such as Flasetto, Tension, and Energy, for adjusting vocal style.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FGEVJRmCBUQQxGIQLqiAd%252Femotion_parameters.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0678101c-7953-430e-a3ff-1ca4db8b937a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3fc50d5&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#parameters)

Parameters

Air[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#air)

This is to control the airiness of the vocal. You can make the vocal more raspy or bright by increasing this parameter.

*   You can slightly increase air when it comes to the powerful part.
    
*   We recommend just making a slight change on this, extreme values might result in unexpected performance.
    

Falsetto[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#falsetto)

This is to control the amount of falsetto of the vocal.

*   When the key is low, increasing the falsetto might not bring much falsetto as expected.
    
*   If you want more falsetto, we recommend decreasing tension at the same time for a better result.
    
*   We recommend just making a slight change on this, extreme values might result in unexpected performance.
    

Tension[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#tension)

This is to control the softness of the vocal.

*   Lower this value, the vocal will be softer. Increase this value, the vocal will be tight.
    
*   We recommend just making a slight change on this, extreme values might result in unexpected performance.
    

Energy[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#energy)

This is to control the power of the vocal.

*   This parameter is not just volume of the sound.
    
*   If you want a gentle sound, we recommend decreasing tension at the same time.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#editing-envelopes)

Editing Envelopes


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Editing an Emotion Control envelope in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FoQKvmOiyrjCqxQuxyDv9%252Fedit_evelopes.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6dc72ae-9f6f-4ffe-88d9-7c52fe028847&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0044031&sv=2)

You can modify the envelope for each parameter by default. There are 4 tools at left side for editing the envelop.

*   Lifting tool - drag vertically to increase or decrease the value. You can modify a certain range by creating a selection on the grid. Hold Shift to modify the whole range of the clip.
    
*   Brush - You can directly draw the envelope. Use right click to erase.
    
*   Eraser - You can erase the envelope back to value 1x.
    
*   Line tool - drag to create a straight line for the envelope.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#editing-real-parameters)

Editing Real Parameters


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Using the 'Real Parameter' mode in ACE Studio to directly edit the generated vocal synthesis data.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FaI5PEN14xIdOYmr0Se7Q%252Fedit_real_parameters.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd7b9397-9625-4d12-bdc3-8601193014dc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4a0315bf&sv=2)

Click on the “Par.” button at left to switch to real parameter mode. You can directly change the parameter.

Just like AI pitch, the real parameters are generated by AI based on the singing style of the current AI voice, melody, lyrics, and pitch. Any changes to these elements will result in the regeneration of each parameter. AI generates AI parameters piece by piece, even you just change one lyric in a piece, all AI parameters in this piece will be regenerated. These parameters are like representations of the audio waveform in different dimensions.

We recommend just modify the envelopes in most of the case. If you want a precise value, you can edit under this mode.

*   Lifting tool - drag vertically to increase or decrease the value. You can modify a certain range by creating a selection on the grid. Hold Shift to modify the whole range of the clip.
    
    *   By using this tool, the part you change will become user parameter, so they will not change after doing any changes on the original elements.
        
    
*   Brush - You can directly draw the envelope. Use right click to erase.
    
    *   By using this tool, the part you change will become user parameter, so they will not change after doing any changes on the original elements.
        
    
*   Eraser - You can erase the envelope back to AI parameter.
    
*   Line tool - drag to create a straight line for the envelope.
    
    *   By using this tool, the part you change will become user parameter, so they will not change after doing any changes on the original elements.
        
    
*   Fixed brush - just AI pitch, you can lock down some parts of the parameter, so they won’t change after doing any changes on the original elements.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls/emotion-controls#formant)

Formant


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Formant is a basic parameter of sound design.

*   Higher this value, the vocal will become more like female or kid.
    
*   Lower this value, the vocal will become heavier.
    

[PreviousVocal Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls)
[NextBreath](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath)

Last updated 2 months ago

# How to Create a Children's Choir | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

In ACE Studio, you can easily create a rich and natural-sounding children's choir using the powerful AI Choir feature. This guide will walk you through the process step-by-step.

1

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-create-a-childrens-choir#enable-choir-mode)

**Enable** [**Choir Mode**](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)

First, lay down the foundation for your choir.

1.  Create a vocal track and input the main melody and lyrics.
    
2.  From the Voice Library, drag a child's voice model (e.g., Xi Lei, Xi Tian, or Qi Xuan) onto the track header.
    
3.  Click the track header to open the track panel. Inside the panel, click the **Turn on Choir Mode** button.
    

2

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-create-a-childrens-choir#build-your-childrens-choir)

**Build Your Children's Choir**

Once Choir Mode is active, you can add and arrange your singers.

*   **Add Members:** Click the **\+ Add** button within the choir panel to duplicate the current singer, instantly increasing the size of your choir.
    
*   **Introduce Variety:** Drag different child voice models from the Voice Library directly into the choir panel. Mixing different voices will create a more diverse and realistic texture.
    
*   **Arrange Singers:** Simply drag the voice avatars within the panel to reorder them.
    

3

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-create-a-childrens-choir#fine-tune-for-a-natural-sound)

**Fine-Tune for a Natural Sound**

Adjust choir settings to make your choir sound more human and spacious.

*   **Offset:** Adjusts slight timing differences between the voices, mimicking the natural imperfections of a real choir for a fuller sound.
    
*   **Spread:** Controls the stereo width of the choir. Increase it to make the choir sound wider and more encompassing.
    
*   **Gain:** Sets the volume for each individual choir member. You can click on a voice avatar to adjust its specific gain level.
    
*   **Effects:** To place your choir in a realistic space, we recommend enabling the Room effect. This adds reverb and creates a sense of depth. To learn more, please refer to .
    

4

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-create-a-childrens-choir#create-harmonies-multi-part-choir)

**Create Harmonies (Multi-part Choir)**

A single choir track acts as one harmony part (e.g., the sopranos). To build a full, multi-part arrangement, you'll need multiple choir tracks.

1.  Right-click your completed choir track and select **Create vocal doubles**. This is better than simply duplicating, as it creates new tracks with subtle, natural variations, avoiding audio phasing issues.
    
2.  Select the MIDI clips on the newly created tracks.
    
3.  Edit the notes in these clips to write your harmony parts (e.g., alto and tenor lines).
    

Now, when you press play, you'll hear a full, multi-part children's choir singing in harmony.

5

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-create-a-childrens-choir#save-your-choir-as-a-preset)

**Save Your Choir as a Preset**

If you've created a choir configuration you love, save it for future use.

In the track panel menu, you can **Save the current choir as a preset**. You can customize its name and tags for easy retrieval. Your saved preset will appear in the **Choir tab** of the Voice Library, ready to be dragged and dropped into any project.

6

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-create-a-childrens-choir#advanced-customizing-timbre-with-blend-voices)

Advanced: Customizing Timbre with Blend Voices

For ultimate control, you can create unique voices for each member of your choir.

In the track panel, select a choir member and expand the **Blend Voices** section. Here, you can mix multiple voice models together to design a completely new, custom timbre for that specific singer. Repeat this for other members to build a choir with unparalleled vocal diversity.

To learn more, please refer to [Voice Blending](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/voice-blending)
.

[PreviousHow to Fine-tune the Pitch Curve](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-fine-tune-the-pitch-curve)
[NextAdd Vibrato or Remove AI-generated Vibrato](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/add-vibrato-or-remove-ai-generated-vibrato)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Expression Controls | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/expression-controls#what-are-expression-controls)

What Are Expression Controls


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Expression Controls are parameters you can automate over time to add nuance and realism, allowing you to "paint" where an effect should be active.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/expression-controls#available-controls)

Available Controls

Vibrato[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/expression-controls#vibrato)

Vibrato is a subtle and rapid fluctuation in a note's pitch, which adds warmth, expression, and richness to the sound.

Split-tones[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/expression-controls#split-tones)

Split-tones are an advanced technique that creates a rough, textured sound by producing multiple pitches simultaneously. It's perfect for adding a raw, edgy character or a sense of tension to your melody.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/expression-controls#editing-expression-controls)

Editing Expression Controls


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FgxWb4Y6YdAaRYsH2Q7tl%252Fexpression_control.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0769fdd-d9c0-4ef9-8298-45c7bda1120e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=499f2d57&sv=2)

1.  Select the Expression Control below the piano roll.
    
2.  Click and drag to "paint" the regions to activate.
    
3.  Simply right-click and drag over an active region to erase it.
    

[PreviousArticulations](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations)
[NextEnsembles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles)

# Mixer | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

The Mixer provides detailed controls for every track in your project. It's a panel that expands from the left side of the track list, giving you access to volume, panning, effects, and routing for each track.

To open or collapse the Mixer, click the Mixer icon in the main toolbar, or use the shortcut M.

![Open Mixer panel in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FhYpYNm3Lv2mEIo2paI8W%252Fmixer.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86a5094b-9088-43ce-857c-d89358670b75&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e2363da&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer#mix-your-tracks-using-mixer)

Mix Your Tracks Using Mixer


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When the Mixer is open, you will see a channel strip for the Master track and for every track in your project.

Master Track is always located at the very top of the Mixer. It controls the overall output volume of your entire project and features a single volume fader.

Track Channels Below the Master Track, each track has its own channel strip with the following controls:

*   Fader: Controls the track's volume. Drag the fader up or down to adjust the level. Double-click the fader to reset it to 0 dB.
    
*   Pan: Adjusts the track's position in the stereo field (left or right). Drag the knob left or right. Double-click to reset it to the center.
    
*   Solo S: Mutes all other tracks, allowing you to hear only soloed tracks. You can solo multiple tracks at once by holding Ctrl / Command.
    
*   FX: Opens the Effects Panel for this track.
    
*   Input Channel: Selects the audio or MIDI source for the track. The available options depend on the track type:
    
    *   For Audio Tracks: Choose from the available input channels of your connected audio interface.
        
    *   For MIDI Tracks: Select a connected MIDI device and a specific MIDI channel. You can choose between Polyphonic and Monophonic input modes in vocal tracks.
        
    

[PreviousMixing](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing)
[NextEffects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Song Writing | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

In ACE Studio, you can easily write songs. Start by preparing and importing chords or beats, then record your hummed melodies. Next, AI tools will convert your audio into MIDI and lyrics. Finally, meticulously edit the lyric content to help you craft perfect original works.

1

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/song-writing#block-dce54bd96e1c4777be509cfb384102b6)

Prepare your chords or beat

You can prepare a beat track on your DAW, and import the beat track back to ACE Studio. (Remember to set up the same tempo) Or you can just create [chord](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track)
 progressions inside ACE Studio.

2

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/song-writing#block-17708bffde8080ac98c9d5b14558622f)

Record your humming

With chords or beat set up, you can [record](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record)
 your humming inside ACE Studio.

3

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/song-writing#block-17708bffde8080fb906af5a7386837e9)

Test and fine-tune your melody

Based on your recordings, you can convert them into MIDI and lyrics with our “[Vocal to MIDI and lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics)
” tool. Then you can edit the melody and lyrics in the piano roll, and hear the vocal result with our AI voices.

4

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/song-writing#block-17708bffde80805db3d1dd5a77373bb5)

Build lyrics on it

Now you have the perfect topline, it’s time to build lyrics on it. You can edit lyrics line by line, or use the lyrics panel to edit whole lyrics together in the lyrics editor window.

To learn more details about editing lyrics, please refer to [Editing Notes](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes)
.

If you want others to write the lyrics, you can save the project and send the project pack to them. Just remember to move your audio files under the “samples” folder. For more details, please refer to [File Management](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management)
.

[PreviousChoir Rehearsal](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/choir-rehearsal)
[NextHow to Fine-tune the Pitch Curve](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/advanced-techniques-and-pro-tips/how-to-fine-tune-the-pitch-curve)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Ensembles | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles#what-is-ensemble)

What Is Ensemble


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ensemble is a feature that allows you to combine multiple AI instruments into one track, organizing them into a cohesive instrumental group.

You can manually save your customized ensemble presets into the Instrument Library, and several pre-made presets are also available.

To use an ensemble preset, simply drag it to the canvas or onto the track head.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles#use-ensemble)

Use Ensemble


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FYFEGK2AeF5nxv2rvywPO%252Fturn_on_ensemble.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D859c30a6-074f-4fb0-b124-f2a4d7bef16d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2cdb4cc&sv=2)

To use ensemble, click the Turn on Ensemble button in the instrument track panel. Disabling ensemble mode will erase all ensemble settings.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles#add-remove-instruments)

Add/Remove Instruments

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F8alsfO0zcJhaT7VtxhxI%252FClipboard-20251029-102746-306.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1089729e-45bd-4ac1-8df8-cc0970ed6bdf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d5572e6&sv=2)

*   Click the \+ Add button to duplicate existing instruments.
    
*   Drag new instruments from the Library to add them to the ensemble.
    
*   Arrange the order of instruments by dragging them.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles#parameter-editing)

Parameter Editing

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FCFFWYQDg9WzvHR2aKvtX%252Fedit_ensemble_parameters.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D660028ea-549e-4ed2-a428-22133f8c0683&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4a568d04&sv=2)

*   Spread: Controls the width of the ensemble sound.
    
*   Offset: Adjusts slight timing differences between instruments for a more natural effect.
    
*   Gain: Sets the volume for individual instruments.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles#effects-for-ensemble)

Effects for Ensemble


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to create a sense of space, we recommend enabling the Room effect.

To learn more about effects, please refer to [Effects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles#save-as-a-preset)

Save as a Preset


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FvASqpOiuyieB5t8jj7GY%252Fsave_ensemble_preset.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8409359c-5756-4d5b-940e-9cf94f03f920&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc46d8c6&sv=2)

In the track panel menu, you can save the current ensemble as a preset. You can customize the preset's name and tags for easy retrieval. Your ensembles preset will be saved in the Ensemble tab of the Instrument Library.

The presets you save will be stored in the cloud and linked to your account.

[PreviousExpression Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/expression-controls)
[NextTransport](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport)

# Transport | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#tempo)

Tempo


----------------------------------------------------------------

![Adjusting tempo in ACE Studio transport.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FxYK5LUb3NFMVJYOFtWd4%252Ftempo.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6849240-5039-4b2f-8989-2531cb0eda2a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2200a60&sv=2)

Drag to set the current tempo according to the position where your timeline is. (For multi-tempo projects, adjusted tempo will only be applied for the section where your timeline is in.)

Double click to type in the exact number of tempo.

ACE Studio supports a tempo range of 1-360 bpm.

If your project involves tempo changes, please refer to [Tempo & Signature Change](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#time-signature)

Time Signature


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FS1KiZlMLnET2Kthz0xC3%252Ftime_signature.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df42a234d-0ca8-4467-bfe5-71efec08bfb7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=300c5886&sv=2)

Drag to set the current time signature according to the position where your timeline is. (For multi-signature projects, adjusted signature will only be applied for the section where your timeline is in.)

Double click to type in the exact number of signature.

If your project involves time signature changes, please refer to [Tempo & Signature Change](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#playback-record-controls)

Playback/Record Controls


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FLF6NFtUzCvu8lj8MZDap%252Fplayback_control.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D898a3c73-91ad-4362-94c7-0c30f29d6432&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8310dd66&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#block-17208bffde8080b5a572c96b9713dbf1)

Back to start

Click to jump the timeline back to the beginning of the project.

*   Shortcut key Enter
    

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#block-17208bffde8080939d09d25c8cdc0e62)

Play/stop

Click to start or stop the playback.

*   Shortcut key Space
    

The playback will always start from the marker-line. If you stop the playback and play again, the playback will still start from the the same start position as last time, unless you relocate the marker-line.

To continue the playback from where you stopped, use shortcut Shift + Space.

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#block-17208bffde8080bbb358d87884dca6ea)

Record

Click to start/end recording.

*   Shortcut key R
    

If the playback is not started, start recording will also start the playback. You can also start recording during the playback.

For more detailed information about Record, please refer to [Record](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#metronome)

Metronome


------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click to turn on/off the metronome.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#loop)

Loop


--------------------------------------------------------------

Click to toggle loop mode on or off.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#loop-brace)

Loop Brace

When loop mode is enabled, loop brace will appear on the time ruler. You can adjust the length of the loop brace by dragging its edges or reposition it by dragging directly. You can also click on the loop brace to turn on/off the loop mode.

After selecting a region, use the shortcut Ctrl/⌘Command+L to turn the selected area into a loop brace. Press the shortcut again to exit loop mode.

When exporting audio, select Export Range as Loop to export the audio within the Loop Brace range. For more details, please refer to [Export Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#auto-scrolling)

Auto Scrolling


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click this trigger to toggle auto-scrolling on or off. During playback, the Arrangement View and Clip View will automatically scroll when the timeline reaches the end of the visible area.

During playback, auto-scrolling will be temporarily disabled if you manually scroll the view until next playback. You can turn it on by clicking.

You can set scrolling animation in Preferences. For more details, please refer to [Preferences](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/transport#timecode)

Timecode


----------------------------------------------------------------------

This shows the time position of time-line.

[PreviousEnsembles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles)
[NextArrangement in Canvas](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas)

Last updated 2 months ago

# AI Choir | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir#what-is-ai-choir)

What Is AI Choir


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

AI Choir is a feature that allows you to combine multiple AI voices into one track, organizing them into a choral part.

You can manually save your customized choir presets into Voice Library. We also provide several pre-made presets.

To use a choir preset, simply drag it to the canvas or onto the track header.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir#choir-mode)

Choir Mode


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir#enable-disable-choir-mode)

Enable/Disable Choir Mode

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FfIIam3wRO7DMYkkhF2k4%252FClipboard-20251029-101657-003.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f7348a9-d8c3-4f1d-8a20-3e61fa175cfb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10ab91dd&sv=2)

Click on the track header of a vocal track to open the track panel. To enable choir mode, click the Turn on ChoirMode button in the track panel. Turning off choir mode will erase all choir settings.

You can also right-click on a vocal track and select "Turn into a choir track".

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir#add-remove-voices)

Add/Remove Voices

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FVokrB9jt2a4ziNYtb7ZQ%252FClipboard-20251029-102353-420.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db871b4cf-e72a-4fd5-9b49-2736a87e5f1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d4f00a69&sv=2)

*   Click the \+ Add button to open the Voice Library, then click on a voice to add it to the choir.
    
*   Right click on a voice to duplicate or delete it.
    
*   Arrange the order of voices by dragging them.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir#editing-parameters)

Editing Parameters

![Adjusting AI Choir parameters like Offset and Spread in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FqhhekxivviP25mEyJmLF%252Fchoir_edit.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e074c5f-4b48-41c6-8e66-585c9526b991&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b2ca0624&sv=2)

*   Offset: Adjusts slight timing differences between voices for a more natural effect.
    
*   Spread: Controls the width of the choral sound.
    
*   Gain: Sets the volume for individual choir members under the voice avatar.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir#effects-for-ai-choir)

Effects for AI Choir


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to create a sense of space or use it for backing vocals, we recommend enabling the Room effect.

To learn more about effects, please refer to [Effects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir#save-as-a-preset)

Save as a Preset


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Saving a custom AI Choir configuration as a reusable preset in the ACE Studio Voice Library.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F7AgojmSz2djMcwyecWBA%252Fchoir_preset.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8857a746-2908-4c62-a618-6bb8c415a556&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7f37227d&sv=2)

In the track panel menu, you can save the current choir as a preset. You can customize the preset's name, tags, and language for easy retrieval. Your choir preset will be saved in the Choir tab of the Voice Library.

The presets you save will be stored in the cloud and linked to your account.

[PreviousSinging Languages](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/singing-languages)
[NextVoice Blending](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/voice-blending)

Last updated 14 days ago

# Voice Blending | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/voice-blending#what-is-voice-blending)

What Is Voice Blending?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With this feature, you can blend different voices to create a hybrid voice by AI.

Voice blending allows you to combine multiple voice seeds under the same vocal synth model version.

You can manually save your customized blended presets into Voice Library.

To use a blended preset, simply drag it to the canvas or onto the track header.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/voice-blending#blending-voices)

Blending Voices


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the track header to open the track panel. There is a module called "blend voice" in the track panel.

*   Click the + button to add different voice seeds from the pop-up list.
    
*   Adjust the blending ratio by dragging vertically on each fader.
    
*   Right-click on a seed to delete or copy it.
    
*   Copy and paste the blending recipe to another singer track using the settings menu at the top-right corner of the panel.
    

![Creating a hybrid AI voice in ACE Studio using the Voice Blending panel to mix multiple singers.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FIEmUvd6lSK9EAcVMFk34%252Fblendvoices.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6209018a-7104-4456-a3db-abcac896be15&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58ef6801&sv=2)

In Verse24 and earlier, blending involves two separate dimensions: Timbre and Style. By default, their ratios are synced. You can un-sync by clicking the chain button in the middle of each seed for independent adjustments.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/voice-blending#blending-voices-in-choir)

Blending Voices In Choir

You can blend voices for each voice within a [choir](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)
. The "Blend voices" module corresponds to the voice selected in the choir member list.

[PreviousAI Choir](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)
[NextInstrument Library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Stem Splitter | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/stem-splitter#what-is-stem-splitter)

What Is Stem Splitter


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Stem Splitter is a tool that allows you to split an audio clip containing a full mix into separate tracks for its core components, such as vocals, drums, bass, and other instruments.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/stem-splitter#how-to-use-stem-splitter)

How to Use Stem Splitter


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Stem Splitter operates on a selected region of your timeline. Click and drag on the Canvas to create a selection. Ensure this selection covers the audio clip you wish to split.

There are 3 ways to open the Stem Splitter panel:

*   Click the **Stem Splitter** icon in the main toolbar.
    
*   With your region selected, right-click on it to open the context menu. Navigate to the AI Tools submenu and select **Stem Splitter**.
    
*   Click on the Split into Stems button at the left side of audio clip viewer. For more information about audio clip, please refer to [Clips](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips)
    .
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/stem-splitter#split-stems)

Split Stems


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Inside the Stem Splitter panel, you need to configure how you want to split the audio.

*   Choose one of the 3 stem split modes:
    
    *   Basic: Vocal + Instrumental
        
    *   Professional: Vocal, Drums, Bass, Piano, Guitar, Others
        
    *   Advanced: All detected stems
        
    
*   Remove reverb and backing vocals, avliable in Basic and Professional mode.
    

After selecting the stem split mode, click the Split button. After a few seconds of process, the stems will be added down below the original track.

[PreviousVoice Changer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/voice-changer)
[NextVocal to MIDI & Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Choir Rehearsal | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

ACE Studio can help you efficiently complete the production and rehearsal of choral works.

1

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/choir-rehearsal#block-565d318609c3423cbed367bee6887c94)

Import your MusicXML file

ACE Studio support MusicXML as .mxl or .musicxml. You can directly import the MusicXML file by drag and drop.

Learn more: [Import Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files)
.

2

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/choir-rehearsal#block-17708bffde80808e8d79efde96746f97)

Check all lyrics and musical settings

After importing your MusicXML, check all the lyrics imported from the file, and check if the tempo is right.

If your song has multiple tempos or time signatures, you can create change marks on the time ruler. To learn about how to insert a tempo mark or a time signature mark: [Tempo & Signature Change](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change)
.

Learn more about editing lyrics: [Editng Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics)
.

3

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/choir-rehearsal#block-17708bffde8080108e08cd5ab4b463ec)

Choose AI voices

Choose the right voice for each vocal track by dragging an AI voice from the voice library on the track head.

*   If you don’t want too much vibrato on the vocal, you can use the modulation tool to make the pitch curve more flat. For more details, please refer to [Editing Pitch](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch)
    .
    
*   For a STAB choir, here are some recommendations to our AI voices:
    
    *   Ember Rose - Pop female voice, soprano
        
    *   Clara Epic - Cinematic female voice, soprano
        
    *   Karolyn - Opera female voice, soprano
        
    *   Zalo - Gospel female voice, alto
        
    *   Jessica - Gospel female voice, alto
        
    *   Aaron - Opera male voice, tenor
        
    *   Robert - Opera male voice, baritone
        
    *   Drex L - Pop male voice, tenor
        
    *   Felix - Mexican male voice, baritone
        
    

4

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/choir-rehearsal#block-17708bffde8080868e94de979eae5812)

Share with a link

After fine-tuning your work, click on the Share button at the transport to upload your project as stems and create a link. So you can send this link to all your choir members, and let them rehearse this song with any devices.

Learn more: [Share Projects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/share-projects)

[PreviousEdit Vocal from a Mixed Track](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/edit-vocal-from-a-mixed-track)
[NextSong Writing](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/use-cases/song-writing)

# Mixing | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------

Mixing is the art of blending all your individual tracks—vocals, instruments, and audio clips—into a single, cohesive piece of music. It's where you balance levels, position sounds in the stereo field, and apply effects to bring your song to life.

In ACE Studio, the Mixing section is divided into two main areas:

*   [Mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
    
*   [Effects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects)
    

[PreviousChord Track](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track)
[NextMixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Creating AI Vocals | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

To generate an AI vocal, you will need to load an [AI voice](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library)
 on a track, and create a [clip](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips)
 on this track from the canvas with [MIDI notes](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes)
 and [lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics)
 as its content.

FAQ


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Can I import MIDI or MusicXML files?[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals#can-i-import-midi-or-musicxml-files)

Yes. You can import your MIDI or MusicXML files into ACE Studio. For more information, please refer to [Import Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files)
.

Can I paste the whole lyrics from elsewhere?[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals#can-i-paste-the-whole-lyrics-from-elsewhere)

Yes. You can paste the entire lyrics into your melody using the [Lyrics Panel](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics#edit-with-lyrics-panel)
.

Can I add a breath before a phrase?[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals#can-i-add-a-breath-before-a-phrase)

Yes. You can add breath in the AI parameters panel. For more information, please refer to [Breath](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath)
.

# Chord Track | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

The Chord Track is a special global track designed for creating and playing back chord progressions. It is a permanent part of your project, fixed at the top of the track list.

The track has its own built-in piano sound, so you can hear the chords you create. You can control its playback with its dedicated Mute and Volume controls on the track header and [mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
.

To show or hide the Chord Track, click the Chord Track button in the track list header.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track#create-chords)

Create Chords


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the Chord Track, double-click on the grid where you want your progression to start. This will create a new chord clip, pre-filled with four default chords.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track#edit-chords)

Edit Chords

*   Select a chord within the clip to edit it. The Chord Editor will appear at the bottom.
    
*   In the editor, you can choose a root note and the chord quality (e.g., Major, minor, 7th).
    
*   To set a different bass note (inversion), click the "Bass" button and select a new bass note from the keyboard display.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track#adjust-and-add-chords)

Adjust and Add Chords

*   Drag the right boundary of any chord to change its duration.
    
*   Click the + button that appears when you hover between or after chords to insert a new chord.
    
*   To make the entire chord progression longer, simply drag the right edge of the chord clip itself.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track#chord-loop)

Chord Loop


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you have created a chord progression you like, you can easily loop it.

*   Click the Loop + button located at the top-right corner of the chord clip. This will create the first loop of your progression.
    
*   After the first loop is created, you can simply drag the right boundary of the last looped section to extend the loops further across your timeline.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track#use-chord-progression-as-background)

Use Chord Progression As Background


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Chord Track can serve as a powerful compositional guide by displaying its harmony in the background of the Piano Roll. This helps you write melodies and basslines that are in key with your chords.

When editing notes, locate the Scale Mode setting in the Piano Roll toolbar. Switch the mode from "Scale" to "Chord".

Once enabled, the notes of the current chord from the Chord Track will be highlighted on the Piano Roll grid.

[PreviousTempo & Signature Change](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change)
[NextMixing](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing)

Last updated 3 months ago

# File Management | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management#save-project)

Save Project


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management#save)

Save

Click **Save Project** in the "File" menu to save the current project.

Shortcut key: Ctrl/⌘ Command + S

Regularly save your work to prevent data loss. Make it a habit to use the save shortcut keys during your workflow.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management#save-as)

Save as

Click **Save as** in the "File" menu to save the project as a new file.

Shortcut key: Ctrl/⌘ Command\+ Shift + S

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management#auto-save)

Auto save

During project startup, an automatic backup will be made every 10 seconds. The automatic backup will be cleared after a manual exit, but will be preserved in case of unexpected crashes. The ACE Studio will proactively ask if you want to open the backup project at the next launch.

Each time you save this project manually, a copy will be saved under this project folder “autosave”. This become a part of the project history, and you can restore a historic version from this folder.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management#collect-all-files-and-save)

Collect all files and save

Click **Collect all files and save** in the "File" menu to copy all audio files from external sources used in the project into the "Samples" folder inside the project folder.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management#project-file-and-project-folder)

Project File and Project Folder


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The project will be saved as a folder in the specified directory, which includes:

*   Project file \*.acep
    
*   "autosave" folder containing automatic backups during project startup and the last 10 historical manually saved backups.
    
*   “Samples” folder containing all audio files generated from this project.
    
    *   You can move the audio files under this folder. If the original audio file path is lost when the project is restarted, ACE Studio will automatically look for it in the project directory. This also helps when sharing the whole folder to others.
        
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management#limits)

Limits


------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The max duration of a project is 40 mins.
    
*   The max number of AI voices in a project is 60.
    

[PreviousEffects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects)
[NextImport Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Publishing Cloned Voice | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/publishing-cloned-voice#what-is-voice-publishing)

What Is Voice Publishing?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want your voice to be seen by producers all over the world, you can publish your voice to the Creative Library.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/publishing-cloned-voice#how-to-publish-my-voice)

How to Publish My Voice?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To publish your voice, click on the Share button on your trained voice. After creating a profile of your voice, the application will be sent to the Creative Library team. For the quality of the creative library, the team will review your voice and decide wether to approve it.

Please note: all voices published to the creative library should be royalty-free.

# Voice Changer | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/voice-changer#what-is-voice-changer)

What Is Voice Changer


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Voice Changer is a tool that allows you to transform the voice in a vocal track into another voice or even into the sound of instruments. The voice changer not only alters the timbre but also adjusts certain stylistic elements, while keeping the melody and lyrics unchanged.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/voice-changer#how-to-use-voice-changer)

How to Use Voice Changer


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Voice Changer operates on a selected region of your timeline. Click and drag on the Canvas to create a selection. This defines the exact region you want to apply the voice changer effect to.

There are 2 ways to open the Voice Changer panel:

*   Click the **Voice Changer** icon in the main toolbar.
    

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fqdt51RKv0dPevUDanHAH%252Fvoicechanger_1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7df8ddd-a160-43db-9b35-4e84ae5eb0fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=569c24ff&sv=2)

*   With your region selected, right-click on it to open the context menu. Navigate to the AI Tools submenu and select **Voice Changer**.
    

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FPJB0NxUWIzH9iY250EuQ%252Fvoicechanger_2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a302cbe-6dd8-493b-9e28-ac76642459f4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d89bdde4&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/voice-changer#voices)

Voices


-----------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FGpIAtmVDNchvpI3KIcsv%252Fvoicechanger_3.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45931c73-e82d-45f7-a5d7-bacba5bcd404&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c76f505&sv=2)

The Voice Changer panel list is divided into three tabs:

*   **Voices:** Contains all pre-made voice changer voices that transform the source into the target singing voice.
    
*   **Instruments:** Contains all pre-made voice changer instruments that transform the source into target instrument sounds.
    
*   **Cloned:** Contains all your customized voice changer voices and instruments. To learn more about cloning your voice for Voice Changer, please refer to [Cloning A Voice for Voice Changer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer)
    .
    

Click on the search bar to activate the search mode. Each voice/instrument is annotated with a name and several tags. You can search with text to locate a voice/instrument you want.

To select a Voice Changer target, click on it. You can select multiple voices and instruments to convert in one batch. Click it again to deselect.

Click on the picture of a voice or instrument to preview its sound.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/voice-changer#settings)

Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FYP1iwwBDB4rPxcbpeLO6%252Fvoicechanger_4.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa305da7-192f-4ad8-a2a3-fec95b3a4078&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aee3cb65&sv=2)

Once a voice/instrument is selected, you can click the settings button to adjust the following parameters:

*   Semitones: Adjust the pitch in semitone increments.
    
*   Pitch correction: Perform pitch correction on the audio.
    
*   Correct by scale: Perform pitch correction based on the specified scale. You can select the scale type and mode.
    
*   Random offset: Add random time offset in milliseconds.
    

Check **Remove instrumental** remove the instrumental part of the source content before conversion.

Check **Remove reverb and harmonies** to remove reverb and harmonies from the source content before conversion.

Click Cancel to undo the current setting changes and close the panel. Click **Apply all** to apply the settings to all related audio clips. Click **Apply** to apply the settings to the currently selected audio clip.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/voice-changer#convert)

Convert


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FaMnOyvVYq3tcpHe0ORpq%252Fvoicechanger_5.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1ee992b-f652-4b9c-bc4c-fc0bbd469ad5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6223e99e&sv=2)

After selecting target voices or instruments, click the Convert button to begin the conversion. Converted clips will appear below the timeline.

If you want to convert to instrument sounds, please note that regular singing vocals as the input source may not produce ideal instrument sounds due to the significant differences in their expressive forms. It is recommended to use vocal audio that mimics instrument sounds for better conversion results.

To create custom Voice Changer voices and instruments, please refer to [Cloning A Voice for Voice Changer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer)
.

[PreviousLocal Rendering](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering)
[NextStem Splitter](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/stem-splitter)

# Arrangement in Canvas | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

The **Canvas** is the arrangement area in ACE Studio. Here, you can create, place, move, and edit all contents as clips along the timeline to create your music works.

In the canvas, each row is a track, and clips can be placed on the grid area. The interaction method of the canvas is based on selection areas, not object selection.

# Cloud Rendering | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Cloud Rendering enables users to process all rendering tasks via cloud servers, ensuring consistent performance regardless of local device specifications.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/cloud-rendering#rendering-timing)

Rendering Timing


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cloud rendering starts when playback is triggered. Some parameters like AI-pitch are pre-rendered when corresponding edit tools are activated.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/cloud-rendering#rendering-state)

Rendering State


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Un-rendered pieces are marked with a gray brace inside the time ruler.

A clip will pulse if it's being rendered.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/cloud-rendering#rendering-scope)

Rendering Scope


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verse25 and later

Verse24 and earlier

The model dynamically detects the rendering range. When a small area is modified, only the modified area will be re-rendered.

The model renders piece by piece. The length of each piece is roughly equivalent to a musical phrase (When the phrase if longer than 15s, it will be split). When a change made in a piece or a connected piece, it will be re-rendered.

[PreviousShare Projects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/share-projects)
[NextLocal Rendering](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Samples | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Creative Library Samples are editable vocal/instrument clips created by the community, designed to streamline the process of music production. Each sample is a MIDI clip that includes lyrics, melody, and AI parameters.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/samples#browse-samples)

Browse Samples


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FsdOqYILCDt9653wWbhpU%252Fsample_lib.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e448daa-760e-4cee-b72a-7f3861c9c155&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef35d209&sv=2)

*   Click on the last icon from the Toolbar to open the Creative Library panel. Navigate to the Sample Clips tab in the Creative Library panel.
    
*   By default, all community-made samples are displayed, sorted by the community list order. Click the sample picture to preview the sample sound.
    
*   Use the Search bar to enter search mode and filter samples based on various criteria, including genre, duration, key, language, and BPM.
    
*   Click on My Collection to view only the samples you’ve collected.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/samples#collect-samples)

Collect Samples


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Uncollected samples are marked with a + icon. Click + to add the sample to your collection.
    
*   Collected but not downloaded samples are marked with a Download button. Click the button to download the sample.
    
*   You can drag collected and downloaded samples directly into your project or click them to use.

# Doubles | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/doubles#what-is-doubles)

What Is Doubles


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In vocal producing, we usually like to record two more takes on the sides panned anywhere from 50%-100% with a lead vocal or harmony vocal for a wider dimension and fullness.

**Why not duplicate?**

If you just duplicate, the contents will be exactly the same to the original one. In this case, AI will generate the same audio result for the duplicated one, this would cause phase issues.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/doubles#create-doubles)

Create Doubles


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Right click on a MIDI clip or the track head, and select “Create vocal doubles” in the right-click menu to open Doubles panel.

![ACE Studio's vocal double panel.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fi6Du5hrTCm8s3xN4s7Mc%252Fdoubles.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48103520-50c7-4d6b-8a70-02b990ad58cf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5496c2b&sv=2)

In the vocal double panel, you can

*   Set up the similarity with the original content. 100% represents no changes to the original one.
    
    *   The default humanization process includes the duration and position of notes and the duration of consonants
        
    *   85% - 90% is good enough for regular needs.
        
    
*   Wether to apply random effects to the user pitch.
    
    *   This will only take effect on the pitch curves that you draw. The AI-generated default pitch will not be changed by selecting this check box.
        
    
*   Wether to apply random effects to the VoiceMix.
    
    *   If you haven’t blended voices on this track, you don’t need to check this box.
        
    

[PreviousVocal to MIDI & Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics)
[NextCloning A Voice for Vocal Synth](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth)

Last updated 1 month ago
