# Articulations | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#what-are-articulations)

What are Articulations


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Articulations are the different techniques an instrument can use to play a note. For example, a violin can play a note by bowing it smoothly (Legato) or by plucking the string (Pizzicato). By default, AI Instruments use a **Smart** mode, which intelligently analyzes the melody to apply the most suitable articulations. However, you can manually assign a specific articulation to any note for full creative control.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#available-articulations)

Available Articulations

The available articulations vary depending on the instrument.

Smart[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#smart)

The AI automatically chooses the best articulation based on musical context.

General[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#general)

A standard, neutral playing style.

Legato[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#legato)

Notes are played smoothly and connected, with no silence in between.

Glissando[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#glissando)

A continuous slide in pitch from one note to the next.

Pizzicato[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#pizzicato)

The strings are plucked with a finger instead of being bowed.

Tremolo[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#tremolo)

A single note is repeated very rapidly, creating a trembling effect.

Growl[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#growl)

A harsh, raspy, or guttural sound, common in jazz and rock.

Scoop[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#scoop)

Bending up to the target note from a slightly lower pitch.

Arp-fall[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#arp-fall)

A rapid, descending series of notes falling away from the main note.

Mute[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#mute)

The sound is dampened or muted, creating a softer, less resonant tone.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/articulations#editing-articulations)

Editing Articulations


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FaPGck63pvKwFXO1yYUr8%252Farticulations.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db86ab812-84c0-4402-bc2d-42fb50f576dd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bab83197&sv=2)

1.  In the Piano Roll, select one or more notes you wish to modify.
    
2.  Locate the **"Articulation"** dropdown menu in the toolbar above the piano roll.
    
3.  Choose your desired articulation from the list.
    

[PreviousEditing Notes](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes)
[NextExpression Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/expression-controls)

# Effects | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

The FX Panel is where you add and control audio effects for each track.

To open the FX Panel, click the FX button in the track header or [mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
 of the track you want to edit.

*   The FX Panel will open on the side and will remain open as you work.
    
*   The FX Panel displays the effects of the currently selected track.
    
*   To close the panel, click the collapse button in its top-right corner, or click the highlighted FX button on the track again.
    

![Open FX panel in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FCJLKJpIxUURBIfaibCiw%252Feffectpanel.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De346ba34-f510-4830-a783-2cbc27447921&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f93278b6&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects#basic-effects)

Basic Effects


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Basic Effects rack contains a chain of five essential audio processors: **EQ3**, **EQV**, **Compressor**, **De-esser**, and **Reverb**. You can turn the entire rack on or off using the power button next to the "Basic effects" title.

![Basic Effects in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FmJ4ekNzA59vULcRntKkA%252Feffect_pack.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a5269a3-c494-41e0-b971-1b47e8739df8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e35bb9e6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects#eq3)

EQ3

A simple yet effective 3-band equalizer for general tone shaping.

*   **Low**: Adjusts the volume of the bass frequencies.
    
*   **Mid**: Adjusts the volume of the middle-range frequencies.
    
*   **High**: Adjusts the volume of the treble frequencies.
    

Drag each knob clockwise to boost (increase volume) or counter-clockwise to cut (decrease volume) the corresponding frequency band. Double-click a knob to reset it to 0 dB.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects#eqv-vocal-eq)

EQV **(Vocal EQ)**

A preset-based equalizer optimized for vocals. Choose one of the four presets that best suits your track's role in the mix.

*   **Lead**: A standard setting for lead vocals, with a gentle low-cut and high-shelf boost to help it stand out.
    
*   **Bright**: Provides a stronger high-frequency boost and a higher low-cut, ideal for a brighter, more airy vocal sound.
    
*   **Backing**: Designed for backing vocals or harmonies, with reduced low and mid frequencies to prevent clashing with the lead vocal.
    
*   **Choir**: Tailored for choir tracks, featuring a wider high-pass filter to clean up low-end rumble and a focus on clarity.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects#compressor)

Compressor

Reduces the volume difference between the loudest and quietest parts of your audio for a more controlled sound.

*   **Threshold Slider**: Drag the slider to set the level at which the compressor starts working. The meter shows how much the volume is being reduced in real-time.
    
*   **Gain**: After compression, the overall volume might be lower. Use this knob to boost the signal back up.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects#de-esser)

De-esser

Tames harsh "s," "sh," and "t" sounds (sibilance) in vocal recordings.

*   **Threshold Slider**: Sets how sensitive the de-esser is. The more you lower the threshold, the more sibilance will be reduced.
    
*   **Frequency**: Use this knob to pinpoint the exact frequency of the harshness. A common range is between 4kHz and 8kHz.
    
*   **Listen Button**: Click this to temporarily listen to only the frequencies the de-esser is affecting. This makes it much easier to find the right frequency to cut.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects#reverb)

Reverb

Adds a sense of acoustic space to your track.

*   **Preset Selector**: Use the < and \> arrows to cycle through different types of reverb spaces. You can select 4 reverb presets:
    
    *   Room
        
    *   Hall
        
    *   Church
        
    *   Cinematic
        
    
*   **Dry/Wet**: Controls the balance between the original, unprocessed signal ("Dry") and the reverb effect ("Wet"). At 0%, you hear no reverb. At 100%, you hear only the reverb. A setting of 10% means the final sound is 90% dry signal and 10% wet signal.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects#room-effect)

Room Effect


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note: The Room Effect is available exclusively on Singer Tracks.

The Room Effect is a special reverb designed to simulate placing the virtual singers in a physical acoustic space, adding realistic depth and dimension to the choir sound.

This effect relies on a third-party component that you'll be prompted to install when first activating choir mode.

At the center of room effect, there shows the virtual recording space, each spot with color represents one voice in the choir.

*   You can arrange the voice position by dragging. The distance between choir and the dash line is how close to the mic.
    
*   At the right top corner, you can set up the size of the recording room.
    
    *   8m X 8m - Studio room
        
    *   16m X 16m - Choir hall
        
    *   30m X 30m - Church
        
    

[PreviousMixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
[NextFile Management](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Share Projects | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/share-projects#share-projects-as-links)

Share Projects as Links


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Share your ACE Studio project.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FvtLRVLSB59NR8vQYlkBF%252Fshare.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe821908-64c1-4017-bae7-a2336f3d9db6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ebaa8a1&sv=2)

This feature is to export stems with lyrics as a web link. Everyone with this link can preview stems and lyrics on any device.

Click on the “Share” button to start sharing. ACE Studio will render all tracks into separated mp3 files, and upload them on your account cloud.

*   Your cloud storage is not limitless, please check your storage according to your membership.
    
*   You can manage your uploaded projects in your web account center.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/share-projects#rehearsal)

Rehearsal


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fx4YNjRHqFT7pFfBGcTVI%252Fshare_rehearsal_1.avif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75528388-448b-44c7-b35d-c91de7001bf2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0baa97d&sv=2)

The shared project page is a stem player. In this player, you can mute tracks and preview each lyric track as you want.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FB0Mh0X1ddU7UFuQNlmFz%252Fshare_rehearsal_2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb79c942-47d2-46a4-bde3-5bebf16fcd58&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94869479&sv=2)

This is designed for choir rehearsal or demo preview.

# Local Rendering | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#turbo-mode)

Turbo Mode


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Turbo Mode offloads the heavy synthesis steps of Verse25 to your local CPU/GPU, reducing cloud latency and accelerating the overall render time.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#testing-your-device)

**Testing Your Device**

Local rendering consumes a significant amount of local computing power, so it requires a certain level of computer configuration.

During the onboarding setup, ACE Studio will automatically test your device's performance. Turbo Mode will be enabled if your device is supported. You can also manage it in the \[Rendering\] tab of preferences window. To enable Turbo Mode manually, you must pass a performance test.

1

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#run-the-test)

Run the test

In the \[Rendering\] [preference](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences)
 window, click the Run Test button to start the test.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F7e6RUiq8UQB1TKoNwYjO%252Fturbo_test.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db56015c2-441a-47ed-933b-715ba2f9f57d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1aee489a&sv=2)

Close other large programs to avoid misjudgment caused by performance consumption from other software.

2

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#during-the-test)

During the test

Don't close ACE Studio or launch other large programs.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F63GN6NBqgM35dfQbzrbO%252Ftesting_turbo_mode.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8db1b617-247f-497c-9fd5-d4287196880f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82b13df7&sv=2)

3

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#get-result)

Get result

Turbo Mode will be automatically enabled if your device passes the test. Otherwise, ACE Studio will stay in cloud rendering, which is still good.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fm48FyDAqn5GnaogAF76I%252Fenable_turbo_mode.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc248e96f-0ba2-41f1-b926-5a4c02cf77c7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd97db88&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#monitoring-during-rendering)

**Monitoring During Rendering**

If local rendering tasks exceed acceptable time limits, users will be prompted to switch back to cloud rendering.

**For Windows Users with Multiple GPUs**

To ensure Turbo Mode runs with maximum performance, we strongly recommend assigning your dedicated (High-performance) GPU to ACE Studio in Windows settings. This is especially important for laptops.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F0PR9NPdDGxyL3TpqWSvg%252Fwin_GPU_setting.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dccda48a1-49ba-4402-be43-1c55eac8e355&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fb52355&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to Windows **Settings > System > Display > Graphics**.
    
2.  Find **ACE Studio** in the application list. If it's not there, add it manually.
    
3.  Click on ACE Studio, select **Options**, and set the GPU preference to **High performance**.
    

**Update Your Graphics Driver for the Best Experience**

To ensure optimal performance and stability on Windows, we recommend downloading the latest driver from your graphics card manufacturer's website.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#rendering-timing)

Rendering Timing


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#by-default)

By Default

Local rendering starts when playback is triggered.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#pre-rendering)

Pre-rendering

When pre-rendering is enabled, local rendering operates in real-time (after changes).

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#rendering-state)

Rendering State


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Un-rendered pieces are marked with a gray brace inside the time ruler.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering#rendering-scope)

Rendering Scope


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The model dynamically detects the rendering range. When a small area is modified, only the modified area will be re-rendered.

[PreviousCloud Rendering](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/cloud-rendering)
[NextVoice Changer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/voice-changer)

# Import Files | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files#import-audio-files)

Import Audio Files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Drag and drop

Import menu

On the Canvas

Drag and drop the audio file on an audio track or empty track.

Place the marker-line in the position where you want to import the clip on the track, and select "Import" from the "File" menu to import the audio file.

Double click a empty track on Canvas, choose **Import Audio or MIDI** button.

You can import multiple files at the same time. Each file will be placed on one track starting from the track you drop on.

Supported file format: \*.mp3 / \*.m4a / \*.wav / \*.flac / \*.ogg / \*.aac / \*.ape.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files#import-midi-musicxml-ufdata-files)

Import MIDI/MusicXML/Ufdata Files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Drag and drop

Import menu

On the Canvas

Drag and drop a file on any vocal track, instrument track, or empty track.

Place the marker-line at the position where you want to place the clip on the track, then select "Import" from the "File" menu to import a prepared MIDI/musicXML/Ufdata file.

Double click a empty track on Canvas, choose **Import Audio or MIDI** button.

You can import multiple files at the same time. Each file will be placed on one track starting from the track you drop on.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files#multi-channel)

Multi-channel

You can import a file with multiple channels.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files#polyphonic)

Polyphonic

If the content is polyphonic, ACE Studio will, by default, convert all overlapping notes into sustain notes after importing, as a singer track cannot synthesize polyphonic content, just as a human cannot sing in polyphony.

To import polyphonic content, hold Ctrl / ⌘Command while dragging a file into ACE Studio. The content will be split into separate melody tracks.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files#import-in-house-files)

Import In-house Files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files#samples-.clips)

Samples(.clips)

“\*.clips” is the format for samples in [creative library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/samples)
. It contains tracks and clips.

To import a sample(.clips), just simply drag and drop into ACE Studio.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files#templates-.acet)

Templates(.acet)

“\*.acet” is the format for templates in [creative library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/samples)
. It warps the whole ace project folder as a pack.

Tp import a template(.acet), just simply drag and drop into ACE Studio.

[PreviousFile Management](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management)
[NextExport Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Export Files | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files#export-audio-files)

Export Audio Files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the Export button from transport to open the audio export window, you can also find "Export Audio" from the \[File\] menu.

> **Keyboard Shortcuts:**
> 
> Mac: ⌘ Command + Shift + R
> 
> Windows: Ctrl + Shift + R

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FcUZ8fOiwYxF5c3Kxjew0%252Fexport.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De823e5cd-7ffc-49cc-970c-9210d9ae18a0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dea8f67d&sv=2)

You can export selected tracks with a certain time range as audio files in the specified format.

*   Rendered Track:
    
    *   Master - export audio from the master track as one audio file.
        
    *   Selected tracks - export selected tracks one by one as separated files.
        
    *   All individual tracks - export all unmuted tracks one by one as separated files.
        
    
*   Export without vocal effects: turn off all vocal effects when exporting.
    
*   Export Range:
    
    *   Whole Project - export the range of whole project, starting from the beginning, end at the last clip.
        
    *   Loop - export the range of loop brace.
        
    
*   Channels: This setting determines the number of audio channels in the exported file.
    
*   Format: This option lets you choose the file type for your exported audio. Different formats have different characteristics regarding quality and file size.
    
*   SampleRate: Sample rate refers to the number of audio samples captured per second. A higher sample rate can capture more detail and a wider frequency range, resulting in higher fidelity but a larger file size.
    
*   Bit Depth: Bit depth determines the dynamic range of your audio—the difference between the quietest and loudest possible sounds. A higher bit depth provides a greater dynamic range and a lower noise floor.
    

For common music production scenarios:

*   For Highest Quality (Mastering, Archiving, Distribution): For final masters or archiving your project, you need the best possible quality.
    
    Recommendation: .WAV, 44100 Hz/48000 Hz, 24 Bit.
    
*   For Pesonal Listening & Sharing: For everyday use where file size is a consideration, MP3 is the standard.
    
    Recommendation: .MP3, 320 kbps.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files#export-midi-ufdata-files)

Export MIDI/Ufdata Files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FxpDjhpuFwO8uV5o6O6te%252Fexport_midi.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D648825cf-925a-41a4-ac1e-08b6a3e828e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=797b4a7&sv=2)

You can export a selection as a \*.mid or \*.ufdata file by selecting "Export MIDI" in the File menu to bring up the export settings window.

> **Keyboard Shortcuts:**
> 
> Mac: ⌘ Command + Shift + E
> 
> Windows: Ctrl + Shift + E

In addition to exporting notes, you can also decide whether to include lyrics and phonemes in the export settings window. You can also choose to merge multi-track content into one file or export each and every MIDI track one by one.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files#export-in-house-files)

Export In-house Files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files#samples-.clips)

Samples(.clips)

“\*.clips” is the format for samples in [creative library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/samples)
. It contains tracks and clips.

To export a sample, create a selection first, then select “Export selection as vocal sample” from File menu.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files#templates-.acet)

Templates(.acet)

“\*.acet” is the format for templates in [creative library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/samples)
. It wraps the whole ace project folder as a pack.

To export a template, save the project first, then select “Export project as song template” from File menu.

[PreviousImport Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files)
[NextShare Projects](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/share-projects)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Record | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Before recording, please set up the input hardware, sample rate, buffer size.

For more information, please refer to [Preferences](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences)
.

To start recording, click the **Record** button on the transport or press the shortcut key R.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#arm-record)

Arm Record


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In ACE Studio, you don't need to manually arm a track for recording. The track will automatically arm for recording when you select it or place the marker line on it.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#record-from-an-empty-track)

Record from An Empty Track


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FKAiWMBnuJE2OvqAsx5na%252Frecord_popup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daff599a3-a5d3-4b0c-ae06-45aacf1f1a27&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bb939144&sv=2)

When selecting an empty track and starting recording, a dialog will appear asking you to choose whether to record Audio or MIDI.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#record-audio)

Record Audio


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#select-a-target-track)

Select a Target Track

The selected (focused) track is automatically armed for recording. A red dot will appear next to the channel name in the [mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
 or on the track header to indicate it's ready.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#set-input-and-monitoring)

Set Input and Monitoring

Choose the correct input channel in [mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
. By default, monitoring is turned off for audio tracks to prevent feedback. You can manually enable the **Monitor Switch** (headphone icon) in [mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
 if you need to hear the live input signal.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#start-and-stop-recording)

Start and Stop Recording

Place the playhead where you want to start and press the **Record** button R in the transport. Press R again or press the Space to stop both recording and playback.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#record-midi)

Record MIDI


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#select-a-singer-or-instrument-track)

Select a Singer or Instrument Track

Select a singer or instrument track. The selected track is automatically armed for recording, indicated by a red dot.

Note: If you select multiple tracks, only the first selected track will be armed for recording.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#set-input-and-monitoring-1)

Set Input and Monitoring

Choose the correct MIDI input in [mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
. For MIDI tracks, monitoring is enabled by default, allowing you to hear the sound as you play on your MIDI device. A headphone icon will be displayed to indicate that monitoring is active. You can turn off the Monitor Switch (headphone icon) in the [mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#using-the-virtual-midi-keyboard)

Using the Virtual MIDI Keyboard

![ACE Studio's virtual MIDI keyboard.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FZDQ85fOy8NOkxtziqrAP%252Fvirtual_midi_keyboard.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D297adcf2-ed35-4a8e-8010-8284642c1fe5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88e1651&sv=2)

If you don't have a MIDI controller, you can use your computer keyboard as a virtual MIDI input device. Activate it from the menu Edit > Virtual MIDI Keyboard(Shortcut key /).

*   Keys A to L correspond to white keys. Keys W E T Y U correspond to black keys.
    
*   Press Z / X to switch octaves down / up.
    
*   Press C / V to decrease / increase velocity.
    
*   When the virtual keyboard is active, some application shortcuts will be temporarily disabled.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record#start-and-stop-recording-1)

Start and Stop Recording

Place the playhead where you want to start and press the **Record** button R in the transport. Press R again or press the Space to stop both recording and playback.

[PreviousClip Editor](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips/clip-editor)
[NextTempo & Signature Change](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change)

# Canvas | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

**Canvas** is the arrangement area in ACE Studio. Here, you can create, place, move, and edit all contents as clips along the timeline to create your music works.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/canvas#marker-line-and-timeline)

Marker-line & Timeline


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Marker-line is a static vertical line that flashes between white and blue, indicating the starting point for playback or the precise position for editing actions, such as pasting. You can click anywhere on the Time Ruler or on the grid to reposition the Marker-line. When a selection exists on the canvas, the marker-line is always positioned at the left boundary of the selection.

The Timeline is a moving vertical line that indicates the current playback position and only appears when playback begins.

*   Press the Space to start playback from the Marker-line's position.
    
*   Press Shift + Space to resume playback from the last paused position.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/canvas#time-ruler)

Time Ruler


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Time Ruler is located at the top of the Canvas, displaying time in a musical format (bars and beats). It serves several key functions:

*   **Time Display:** Shows the project's timeline in bars and beats.
    
*   **Navigation and zooming:**
    
    *   Drag horizontally on the Time Ruler to scroll the view.
        
    *   Drag vertically on the Time Ruler to zoom the view.
        
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/canvas#grid-and-snap)

Grid & Snap


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Canvas features a background grid that represents musical time divisions, helping you align clips precisely. Editing actions (like moving or trimming clips) will automatically snap to these grid lines by default.

Right-click on the blank area of the Canvas to open the Grid & Snap menu.

*   Auto-Narrow: Automatically adjusts the grid size to narrow spacing based on the zoom level of the Canvas.
    
*   Auto-Medium(default): Automatically adjusts the grid size to medium spacing based on the zoom level of the Canvas.
    
*   Auto-Wide: Automatically adjusts the grid size to wide spacing based on the zoom level of the Canvas.
    
*   1-16 Cell/Beat: Divides each beat into 1-16 grid cell.
    
*   Snap off: Disables snapping to the grid. Allows free placement of clips without alignment to the timeline. You can also bypass it by holding down the Ctrl/ ⌘Command while editing.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/canvas#navigating-and-zooming)

Navigating & Zooming


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Horizontal/Vertical Scrolling:** Use your mouse wheel to scroll vertically. Hold Shift while using the mouse wheel to scroll horizontally.
    
*   **Zooming:** Hold Ctrl/ ⌘Command and use the mouse wheel to zoom in and out horizontally.
    
*   **Hand Tool:** Hold down the middle mouse button and drag to pan the view in any direction.
    

[PreviousArrangement in Canvas](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas)
[NextTracks](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Cloning A Voice for Voice Changer | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#what-is-voice-changer-cloning)

What Is Voice Changer Cloning?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a feature to customize your own voice changer voice by uploading your samples. AI will learn the timbre based on the samples you upload, and clone a digital version of this voice.

After the customization, you can use your profile to convert voices from audio just like our pre-made AI voice changer voices in ACE Studio.

Your cloned AI voice is private under your account, no one else can access it without your authorization.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#how-to-clone-my-voice-for-voice-changer)

How to Clone My Voice for Voice Changer?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#preparing-your-datasets)

Preparing Your Datasets

Clean Dry Vocals[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#clean-dry-vocals)

High-quality voices require clean and dry vocal samples:

*   Without any reverb, delay, chorus effects
    
*   Without background noise
    
*   Without instrumentals or any non-human sounds
    
*   Without any harmonies or vocal doubles
    

30-100 mins of singing vocal samples are recommended for a voice. The more samples you provide, the more singing details AI can learn, but it brings fewer benefits when you reach over 120 minutes.

> Room Reflections
> 
> Vocals recorded with big room reflections might cause error recognitions and result in unexpected model performances.

> Vocals from stem splitter
> 
> When you are using vocal remover or stem splitter for vocals, the output quality might be damaged too low for training. For a higher quality voice model, please optionally use vocals from stem splitter.

Recording Samples[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#recording-samples)

**Quality microphone with audio interface**

Professional microphones with audio interfaces bring high-quality vocals. You'll need recording software to connect to your interface, record, edit, and mix your vocals.

When recording for a voice model, avoid microphones that are not built for singing:

*   Phone or laptop mics
    
*   Lapel or headset mics
    
*   Karaoke mics
    
*   Earphone mics or bluetooth earphones like air pods (these are usually for phone talks)
    

**Recording environment**

1.  Unwanted background noises can include people talking, electrical hums and buzzes, traffic and outdoor noise, as well as movements of accessories or objects. To prevent these noises from interfering with your recording, it is important to select a quiet location. Choose a place where you can minimize or eliminate unexpected noise disturbances.
    
2.  Sound reflections can occur due to the presence of hard, level surfaces, resulting in reverberation or echoes in your recordings. This can give your tracks a hollow or distant quality, detracting from the desired intimacy and clarity.
    
3.  Try clapping your hands sharply in the room and listen carefully. If you perceive a fluttering sound or a prolonged echo, it indicates the presence of reverb issues.
    
4.  To address this, incorporate soft materials that can absorb sound. Consider using carpets, rugs, or thick curtains to significantly reduce reflections. Covering hard floors and, if possible, hanging curtains over windows, as well as placing furniture with fabric coverings in the room, can be beneficial.
    
5.  Avoid using hard surfaces as they contribute to the problem. If you cannot afford professional acoustic panels, you can utilize everyday items such as canvas paintings, tapestries, or foam tiles to break up these surfaces.
    
6.  When setting up your microphone, be mindful of its placement. Avoid positioning it too close to walls or in corners. Instead, aim for the center of the room or experiment with different locations to find the optimal spot with minimal reverb.
    

**Headphone bleed**

During recordings, particularly when capturing vocals, it is common for the audio from headphones to bleed into the microphone. This issue arises when the volume of the headphones is set too high or when open-back headphones are being used. This might be acceptable when recording for a song, but try to avoid this bleeding when recording for your voice model.

**Microphone placement**

For regular volume, it is recommended to position yourself about 2 inches away from the microphone. However, for louder phrases or when belting, it is advisable to increase the distance to around 4-6 inches. It is important to note that you should always stay closer than 12 inches from the microphone to maintain optimal audio capture.

> Creating Space for Belting
> 
> When engaging in belting techniques, it's important to allow yourself ample space, both in terms of microphone distance and the size of the room you're in. Excessive sound isolation, such as being confined in a closet or booth, or surrounding your microphone with foam, can easily result in overloading the microphone capsule. If you're unsure, it's advisable to incorporate more room sound when performing belted phrases.

Singing Languages[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#singing-languages)

For a voice changer voice, you don’t need to keep all samples in one language.

Singing or Speech[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#singing-or-speech)

For a voice changer voice, there is no big difference between speech samples and singing samples. But for a singing voice changer voice, it is more suitable to use singing samples for training.

File Quality Settings[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#file-quality-settings)

The audio quality of your samples directly impacts the quality of your voice.

We recommend you to set your audio quality in:

*   Bit Depth = 16-bit
    
*   Sample Rate = 44.1khz or 48khz
    
*   Lossless file format (.wav or .flac)
    

Post-Processing[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#post-processing)

To maintain the natural character and clarity of your target voice:

*   **No overlaps:** multi-layered vocals can complicate AI's analysis. Place the overlapped takes at back and stick to a single vocal track to ensure the AI can accurately process and learn from your samples.
    
*   **No hard cuts:** hard cuts can create abrupt starts or ends, which are not normal in a natural singing sound and can introduce clicks or pops. Use smooth fades at the beginning and end of the vocal clip for a more natural transition.
    
*   **No duplicating sections:** Duplicated sections don't help for the training. Your voice model benefits from the natural variation of performance.
    
*   **Control the volume:** Make sure your samples stay around 30-50% of your meter. Use a volume rider or automation to make sure volume levels are consistent across your entire dataset. The aim is to create a consistent volume level across the recording while keeping the dynamics within sections.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#training-your-voice)

Training Your Voice

After preparing your datasets, you can go to [Custom Voice Page](https://acestudio.ai/app/custom-voice/voice-changer)
 to select a Custom Slot, upload your samples, and start the training.

You can customize one voice changer voice in one custom slot.

Click on a slot to start uploading your samples.

After all samples being uploaded, the training will start automatically. You can check its status by refreshing the webpage.

When the page jumps back to the slot list with a new trained voice, you’re all set.

Click ‘Open in ACE’ to open ACE Studio and use your new trained voice.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#re-training-your-voice)

Re-training Your Voice

Click on the Retrain button to retrain your voice.

Retraining will remove your previous voice under this slot. AI will start training a completely new voice from scratch using the new dataset. Prior to initiating the retraining process, you have the option to either retain the historical samples within this slot and upload additional new samples, or you can choose to clear the historical samples and only use the newly uploaded samples.

When preparing new samples, please note:

*   If the duration of newly added samples is significantly smaller than the already uploaded samples, for example, adding 1 min of new sample to a dataset of 30 mins, retraining may not bring about significant changes in the performance.
    
*   Retraining will not change the type of your slot.
    

**When should I retrain my voice?**

*   When your datasets has better quality or larger amount than before, you can use them to iteratively improve your voice
    
*   When you are not satisfied with the current result and want to adjust your datasets
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-voice-changer#managing-your-voice)

Managing Your Voice

Click on the Manage button to open the management window of a custom voice changer voice. In that window, you can modify:

*   Voice picture
    
*   Voice name
    
*   Tags
    
*   Voice type
    
*   Language tag (only for the type of voice)
    

After doing changes, you can click on the Open in ACE button to refresh the voice list of ACE Studio.

[PreviousPublishing Cloned Voice](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/publishing-cloned-voice)
[NextSamples](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/samples)

Last updated 16 days ago

# Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics#what-is-vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics)

What Is Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With this feature, you can convert a vocal track into a MIDI clip with lyrics on each note.

If you want to start your vocal production based on an existing vocal or on the vocal you just recorded, this is the best tool for editing everything of the vocal including melody, lyrics, voice, and emotions.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics#access-vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics)

Access Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 3 ways to convert Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics:

*   Drag and drop an audio clip on a singer track.
    
*   Click the "Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics" button in the left tool panel of the [audio editor](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips/clip-editor)
    .
    
*   Right click on an audio clip, select “Vocal to MIDI & lyrics” from the “AI tools” option.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics#convert)

Convert


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![ACE Studio's Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics tool.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FSUclFSeAxTPafdZdkSbq%252FVocal2midi.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4270749-3771-4f23-8c3a-e21aae757342&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71749309&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics#select-language)

Select Language

In the Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics panel, select the language that matches your content.

Currently, this feature supports lyric recognition in four languages: English, Spanish, Chinese, and Japanese.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics#handling-other-languages-or-extracting-notes-only)

Handling Other Languages or Extracting Notes Only

To convert vocals in other languages to MIDI or extract only the note information (excluding lyrics), choose the "**Note Only**" option from the language selection dropdown menu.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics#use-original-pitch)

Use Original Pitch

Check the box below to retain the original pitch curve from the input vocal. After conversion, the original pitch will be applied as the user pitch in the clip. If you change the lyrics, make sure to erase the pitch curve; otherwise, the pitch may not align with the new lyrics, leading to unnatural pronunciation.

To learn more about pitch curve, please refer to [Editing Pitch](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-pitch)
.

*   This feature is specifically designed for acapella vocals. If the input includes instrumental tracks, delay effects, or reverb effects, accurate conversion may not be guaranteed.
    
*   The converter supports analyzing only one language at a time. If your audio contains multiple languages, please choose the "Note Only" option or split the audio and process each language separately.
    

[PreviousStem Splitter](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/stem-splitter)
[NextDoubles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/doubles)

# Private Share | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/private-share#what-is-voice-private-sharing)

What Is Voice Private Sharing


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can share your cloned voice with other users privately by registering collab seats while remaining all control under your account.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/private-share#register-a-collab-seat)

Register a Collab Seat


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can register a collab seat for any of your cloned voice in the [home page of voice cloning](https://acestudio.ai/app/custom-voice/vocal-synth)
.

To register a seat, just click the Share button on the card of your cloned voice and input the user ID of your collaborator.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/private-share#manage-all-collab-seats)

Manage All Collab Seats


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can manage each seat anytime by changing or clearing the registered user IDs.

All seats are shown in the slot management page.

# Tempo & Signature Change | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

The Tempo and Signature tracks are global tracks that control the project's overall tempo and time signature. They are unique, always docked at the top of the track list.

To show or hide the Tempo and Signature tracks, click the BPM/SIG button in the track list header. This button toggles the visibility of both tracks simultaneously.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change#tempo-changes)

Tempo Changes


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Tempo Track allows you to create dynamic tempo changes throughout your project using an automation lane. It consists of tempo points and the lines that connect them.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change#tempo-points)

**Tempo Points**

A tempo point is a node that defines a specific BPM value at a specific point in time.

*   Adding Points:
    
    *   Click on the curve to create a new tempo point at that position.
        
    *   Click and drag to create a point and immediately adjust its position and BPM value.
        
    
*   Adjusting Points:
    
    *   Drag a point vertically to change its BPM value, or horizontally to change its timing. A point cannot be moved past its adjacent points.
        
    *   By default, points snap to the grid when moved horizontally. Hold Ctrl / ⌘Command while dragging to disable snapping.
        
    *   You can also type in a value in the context menu by right-clicking on a point.
        
    
*   Deleting Points: Double-click a point, or right-click it and select 'Delete' from the menu.
    

Note: Every project starts with a default tempo point of 120 BPM at the beginning. This initial point cannot be moved or deleted, but you can change its BPM value.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change#adjusting-tempo-curves)

Adjusting Tempo Curves

The line between two tempo points represents the tempo transition. By default, this is a linear (straight line) change.

*   Hover over the line segment to reveal a curve handle at its center.
    
*   Drag this handle vertically to adjust the curve, creating a smoother or more abrupt tempo transition.
    
*   Double-click the curve handle to reset the transition back to a straight line.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change#tempo-brush)

Tempo Brush

The Tempo Brush offers a different way to edit tempo by "drawing" it.

*   Click the Tempo Brush icon on the Tempo Track's header to enable it.
    
*   With the brush active, you can click and drag directly on the track to draw a continuous tempo curve. This process creates a series of fine-grained tempo points automatically.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change#adjusting-tempo-curve-limits)

Adjusting Tempo Curve Limits

By default, the tempo curve operates within a display range of **60-180 BPM**.

Should you adjust a tempo point beyond this default range, the upper and lower limits of the display will automatically adapt to accommodate your new tempo point.

For manual control, you can expand the [Mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/mixer)
 panel and directly input your desired upper and lower limits for the tempo curve's display.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FFJf0FBWog9lLSH9dqsz1%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-10-29%252021.19.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41801da9-69a2-46df-be86-b9d9d13f423c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=136e38ea&sv=2)

ACE Studio's supported tempo range for a project is **10-360 BPM**.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tempo-and-signature-change#time-signature-changes)

Time Signature Changes


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Signature Track uses markers to set the time signature for different sections of your project.

Signature Markers are represented as cards that must be placed at the beginning of a measure.

*   Adding Markers: Hover your mouse over the start of a measure that doesn't have a marker. A translucent + icon will appear. Click it to add a new signature marker, which will initially copy the value of the previous marker.
    
*   Adjusting Markers:
    
    *   Drag a marker to move it to a different measure.
        
    *   Click a marker to select it. Once selected, you can copy, paste, or delete it.
        
    
*   Editing Marker Values:
    
    *   Double-click a marker to enter edit mode.
        
    *   You can edit the numerator and denominator separately. Press Tab to switch between the two input fields.
        
    *   Press Enter or click elsewhere to confirm the change.
        
    

Note: Every project starts with a default 4/4 signature marker at the beginning. This marker cannot be moved or deleted, but its value can be edited.

[PreviousRecord](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record)
[NextChord Track](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/chord-track)

Last updated 14 days ago

# Song Templates | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Creative Library Templates are pre-designed song structures created by the community, serving as a foundation for music production. These templates include arrangements, instrumentation, and other key elements, allowing you to build upon existing frameworks.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/song-templates#browse-templates)

Browse Templates


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F6ALCcD03ZMJ4c8KspcUl%252Ftemplate_lib.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc785247b-7ec9-46f5-b6f3-c5f608f44d73&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a1d90f23&sv=2)

*   Click on the last icon from the Toolbar to open the Creative Library panel. Navigate to the Song Templates tab in the Creative Library panel.
    
*   By default, all community-made templates are displayed, sorted by the community list order. Click the template picture to preview the template sound.
    
*   Use the Search bar to enter search mode and filter templates based on various criteria, including genre, duration, key, language, and BPM.
    
*   Click on My Collection to view only the templates you’ve collected.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/song-templates#collect-templates)

Collect Templates


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Uncollected templates are marked with a + icon. Click + to add the template to your collection.
    
*   Collected but not downloaded templates are marked with a Download button. Click the button to download the template.
    
*   Click the collected and downloaded templates to load the template project directly.
    

[PreviousSamples](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/samples)
[NextACE Bridge 2](https://docs.acestudio.ai/daw-integration/ace-bridge-2)

# Make a Vocal in 1 min | Guides | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/make-a-vocal-in-1-min#create-a-vocal-clip)

Create a Vocal Clip


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252F6IxUii5YimiHxEUl2Jrk%252Fbrowse_voice_from_toolbar.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9228a0d4-8946-48e2-8245-9ed24b8a23aa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e29fd64f&sv=2)

Click the first icon (Vocal synth) in the Tool Bar to open the Voice Library. Drag and drop a singer onto the Canvas to create a Vocal Clip. Double-click the Clip to open the piano roll.

You can try different AI voices in the Voice Library. Learn more: [Arrangement in Canvas](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas)
, [Voice Library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/make-a-vocal-in-1-min#input-melodies)

Input Melodies


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252FUDjqQu4b3rzvJfFrRHCA%252Fnote_mover_gif.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9605e855-6547-4484-8153-44442ecdf6d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82e28e8c&sv=2)

By default, your cursor is on “Note Move” mode, which is to select and move notes, but you can create a half-block note by double-click.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252FMrTtecwLRqD8EplvPVYg%252Fnote_brush_gif.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e5ebc42-84f9-40cb-a776-b947ac654d2b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59ac2175&sv=2)

Select the second tool “Note Brush” from the tool bar at top of piano roll, then you can draw notes on the grid by dragging.

You can also input melodies by importing MIDI/MusicXML files, or even an audio file. Learn more: [Editing Notes](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes)
, [Import Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files)
, [Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/make-a-vocal-in-1-min#input-lyrics)

Input Lyrics


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252Fwq1wvm6PuVGF9fvZWgJG%252Fedit_line_by_line.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f78db49-8f1d-4f09-b277-695a50ca2a42&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67af61dd&sv=2)

Click the text line below the notes, then you can type in lyrics into the text-box. Press \[Enter\] or click anywhere on the grid to confirm the lyrics.

Lyrics can be imported from a MIDI/MusicXML/UFdata file. Learn more: [Editng Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editng-lyrics)
, [Import Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/import-files)

In ACE Studio, all of our pre-made AI voices can sing in multilingual, as well as they all have their own native language which they pronounce the best in. Learn more: [Singing Languages](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/singing-languages)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/make-a-vocal-in-1-min#add-a-breath)

Add a Breath


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2505478880-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FeWTNxoktCUvejWVp8Lz9%252Fuploads%252FvAEofmLTiV6lqmz87fWU%252Fbreath.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4559d3ef-28e2-45b0-8a47-edd98a11fb73&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2016ea84&sv=2)

Click the “Breath” tab at the bottom of piano roll, click on the purple area to add a breath at the begining of the melody.

You can fine-tune the vocal performance of AI singers by adjusting Vocal Controls. Learn more: [Vocal Controls](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/vocal-controls)
, [Breath](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/breath)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/make-a-vocal-in-1-min#play-and-export)

Play and Export


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the grid before all notes in piano roll to place the marker-line.

Press Spacebar to start the playback. It will take seconds to render the vocal, when the rendering is done, the playback will continue automatically.

Click the Export button at the top of ACE Studio window.

Choose your preferred format and hit Export to get your audio file.

Learn more: [Export Files](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/file-management/export-files)

This is how easy it is to make a vocal in ACE Studio.

[PreviousBeginner Tutorial](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides)
[NextCreate AI Instrument sounds in 1 min](https://docs.acestudio.ai/guides/for-newcomers/beginner-tutorial/create-ai-instrument-sounds-in-1-min)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Licenses | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/licenses#licenses-for-the-use-of-vocal-synth-voices)

Licenses for the Use of Vocal Synth Voices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/licenses#royalty-free-voices)

Royalty-Free Voices

Most of our pre-made voices are royalty-free. You can check it by hovering your mouse on each AI voice.

If you need a proof of license, just click on the “Generate a certificated license” button in the AI voice profile panel. In the pop up window, you just need to input your name and click generate, a pdf file will be generated for you.

If you need more help with certificates of voice license, please feel free to contact us through [\[email protected\]](https://docs.acestudio.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e0939590908f9294a081838593949584898fce8189)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/licenses#id-3rd-party-license-required-voices)

3rd Party License Required Voices

There are only a few third-party voices that require licenses for commercial use. You can find their profile showing “third-party license required”.

To apply for a license, you can click on the “Learn more” button to find the contacts.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/licenses#licenses-for-the-use-of-ai-instruments)

Licenses for the Use of AI Instruments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each of our pre-made instruments are royalty-free. You can check it by hovering your mouse on each AI instrument.

If you need a proof of license, just click on the “Generate a certificated license” button in the AI instrument profile panel. In the pop up window, you just need to input your name and click generate, a pdf file will be generated for you.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/licenses#voice-changer-voices-instruments)

Voice Changer Voices/Instruments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All of our pre-made voice changer voices/instruments are royalty-free, allowing you to freely use the converted voices for any commercial purposes.

If you need more help with certificates of voice license, please feel free to contact us through [\[email protected\]](https://docs.acestudio.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#cebdbbbebea1bcba8eafadabbdbabbaaa7a1e0afa7)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/licenses#ai-for-music)

AI for Music


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We stand for [**Principles for Music Creation with AI**](https://aiformusic.info/)
**:**

> The Principles for Music Creation with AI establish a guideline for the responsible use of Artificial Intelligence in music. By adopting these principles, companies and organizations commit to protecting the vital contributions of human creativity and to the responsible development and application of artificial intelligence for music creation.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F8IQdMpvY2djAV3vLxNOH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7057501-e9ae-42e9-9926-24c6f0aca40a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3d44365&sv=2)

[NextPhoneme Dictionary](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/phoneme-dictionary)

# 安装 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/an-zhuang#an-zhuang-ace-studio)

安装 ACE Studio


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ACE Studio 是适用于 Windows 和 macOS 的桌面应用。要安装 ACE Studio，请按照以下步骤操作。

1

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/an-zhuang#undefined)

[下载安装程序](https://acestudio.ai/download/)

点击以打开下载页面。

如果您是 Mac 用户，请点击 适用于 Mac 按钮以下载 macOS 的安装程序。

如果您是 Windows 用户，请点击 适用于 Win 按钮以下载 Windows 的安装程序。

2

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/an-zhuang#yi-jian-an-zhuang)

一键安装

下载完成后，打开安装程序（从浏览器的下载列表或“下载”文件夹中）。

安装程序会自动运行，安装 ACE Studio，并在安装完成后启动它。

如果安装失败或 ACE Studio 未启动，请参阅 [Can’t launch ACE Studio?](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-studio-issues/cant-launch-ace-studio)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/an-zhuang#xi-tong-yao-qiu)

系统要求

最低系统版本要求：

*   Windows 10 64 位，版本 1809 或更高
    
*   macOS 11.0 (Big Sur) 或更高版本
    

ACE Studio 需要网络连接才能运行。

通过云端渲染，标准配置的电脑也能轻松运行 ACE Studio。同时我们还提供 Turbo模式 功能，可充分利用电脑的计算能力，在高性能机器上显著提升 AI 渲染速度。更多详情请参阅 [本地渲染](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-xuan-ran/ben-di-xuan-ran)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/an-zhuang#chong-xin-an-zhuang-ace-studio)

重新安装 ACE Studio


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

重新安装前无需卸载。只需下载并打开最新的安装程序 [此处](https://acestudio.ai/download/)
，它会自动更新或重新安装 ACE Studio 到最新版本。

[上一页更新内容](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/geng-xin-nei-rong)
[下一页界面导览](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/jie-mian-dao-lan)

最后更新于2个月前

# Audio Tracks | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/audio-tracks#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When audio clips are present on a empty track, it becomes a Audio Track.

Double-click on the empty area of the track to quickly import audio files. For more information, please refer to [Clips](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips)
.

You can record sounds on Audio Tracks. For more information please refer to [Record](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record)
.

# Clips | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Clips in ACE Studio's Canvas.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FTfy7tXfB39Qkwswf8njF%252Fclips.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa410fa0-563e-402d-938c-4fd206e76c14&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=99acc081&sv=2)

Clips are the basic units on a track that carry audio or MIDI content. Each clip has a title bar with a name on it, and has its body that shows the thumbnail of main content.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#general-editing)

General Editing


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the Canvas, you can edit clips or part of clips within the range of a selection. Click on the title bar of a clip to create a selection that covers the whole range of this clip; Drag out a selection to cover a part of clips that you want to edit. Then you can perform various operations on the clip, such as copying, cloning, and deleting.

Editing content[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#editing-content)

Double click on the body of a clip to open the editor, where you can edit its content.

Moving clips[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#moving-clips)

After creating the selection, drag on the title bar to move the clip. If the selection only covers a part of the clip, this part will be split out while being moved.

Deleting clips[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#deleting-clips)

After creating a selection, you can use Delete to remove the part covered by the selection. If the selection covers an entire clip, the clip will be completely deleted; if the selection only covers part of a clip, the portion of the clip covered by the selection will be trimmed.

Adjusting length[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#adjusting-length)

Clips can have their length adjusted by dragging the left/right edges. You can also create a selection to delete a part of a clip.

Fades & cross-fades[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#fades-and-cross-fades)

When hovering the cursor on a clip, there will be 2 little squares at the top left/right corner of the clip. Drag the square horizontally to create fade in/out for the clip. Drag on the handles on the fade curve to adjust the slope.

When 2 clips are connected, dragging the square across clips will create a cross-fade.

Splitting clips[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#splitting-clips)

There are 2 ways to split clips:

*   Split a clip at a specific position: Place the marker-line at where you would like to split, and use the split function from right-click menu.
    
*   Split out a piece from a clip: Create a selection to cover the piece you would like to split, and use the split function from right-click menu.
    

Shortcut key Ctrl / ⌘Command + E .

Deactivate clips[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#deactivate-clips)

Deactivated clips are in dark color and will not be synthesized or heard.

To deactivate a clip, you can:

*   Click on the title bar of the clip, and deactivate it from right-click menu.
    
*   Place the marker-line within a clip, and deactivate it from right-click menu.
    

To deactivate a piece of a clip, you can:

*   Create a selection to cover the piece you would like to deactivate, and deactivate it from right-click menu.
    

Shortcut key 0.

Changing Colors[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#changing-colors)

The color of a clip follows the color of its current track. You can assign a color for the clip from the right-click menu.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#midi-clips)

MIDI Clips


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A MIDI clip can be created by double-clicking on a vocal/instrument track. You can also import MIDI, MusicXML, UFDATA files as clips.

Vocal Clips

Instrument Clips

General MIDI Clips

Vocal clips contain MIDI notes, lyrics, and Vocal Control parameters.

You can create new or import MIDI files on a Vocal Track to obtain Vocal clips.

Instrument clips contain MIDI notes, articulations and Expression Controls parameters.

You can create new or import MIDI files on an Instrument Track to obtain Instrument clips.

General MIDI clips contain MIDI notes.

You can create new or import MIDI files on an empty MIDI Track to obtain General MIDI clips.

> Type conversion:
> 
> Different types of MIDI clips carry some specific types of information, such as vocal clips containing lyrics and instrument clips containing articulations. When a MIDI clip of a certain type is moved to a track of another type, this specific information will be lost.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips#audio-clips)

Audio Clips


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Audio Clips are imported or recorded audio files contained in an Audio Track.

[PreviousAudio Tracks](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/audio-tracks)
[NextClip Editor](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips/clip-editor)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Tracks | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the Canvas, each row represents a track.

By default, Canvas contains 100 empty tracks. Tracks can hold MIDI Clips, Audio Clips.

Depending on the content loaded on the track, the track types can be categorized as:

*   [MIDI Tracks](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/midi-tracks)
    
*   [Audio Tracks](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/audio-tracks)
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks#general-controls)

General Controls


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each track header has an icon, track name, mute button (triangle), track index, solo button, fx button.

*   Click on any part of the track header except the image to select the track, you can hold Shift to select multiple tracks.
    
    *   Hold Ctrl / ⌘Command to activate multiple solos
        
    
*   Click on the triangle to mute this track.
    
*   Right click on the track header to see all control options.
    
    *   You can delete, copy, cut, and duplicate it, or paste tracks below it.
        
    *   Click rename to edit the track name.
        
    *   Click to turn on [Choir Mode](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)
        /[Enssembles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles)
        , or create [Doubles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/doubles)
        .
        
    
*   You can see the solo button and [FX](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects)
     button by hovering your mouse on a track header.
    

[PreviousCanvas](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/canvas)
[NextMIDI Tracks](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/midi-tracks)
