# Cloning A Voice for Vocal Synth | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#block-17608bffde808018b367cbddf8c9fe36)

What Is Vocal Synth Cloning?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a feature to customize your own vocal synth model by uploading your vocal samples. AI will learn the timbre and singing style based on the samples you upload, and clone a digital version of your voice.

After the customization, you can use your voice to generate vocals from MIDI and lyrics just like our pre-made AI voices in ACE Studio.

Your cloned AI voice is private under your account, no one else can access it without your authorization.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#block-17608bffde8080b98024eb3edc82d4d6)

How to Clone My Voice for Vocal Synth?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#preparing-your-datasets)

Preparing Your Datasets

Clean Dry Vocals[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#clean-dry-vocals)

High-quality voices require clean and dry vocal samples:

*   Without any reverb, delay, chorus effects
    
*   Without background noise
    
*   Without instrumentals or any non-human sounds
    
*   Without any harmonies or vocal doubles
    

30-100 mins of singing vocal samples are recommended for a voice. The more samples you provide, the more singing details AI can learn, but it brings fewer benefits when you reach over 120 minutes.

> Room Reflections
> 
> Vocals recorded with big room reflections might cause error recognitions and result in unexpected model performances.

> Vocals from stem splitter
> 
> When you are using vocal remover or stem splitter for vocals, the output quality might be damaged too low for training. For a higher quality voice model, please optionally use vocals from stem splitter.

Recording Samples[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#recording-samples)

**Quality microphone with audio interface**

Professional microphones with audio interfaces bring high-quality vocals. You'll need recording software to connect to your interface, record, edit, and mix your vocals.

When recording for a voice model, avoid microphones that are not built for singing:

*   Phone or laptop mics
    
*   Lapel or headset mics
    
*   Karaoke mics
    
*   Earphone mics or bluetooth earphones like air pods (these are usually for phone talks)
    

**Recording environment**

1.  Unwanted background noises can include people talking, electrical hums and buzzes, traffic and outdoor noise, as well as movements of accessories or objects. To prevent these noises from interfering with your recording, it is important to select a quiet location. Choose a place where you can minimize or eliminate unexpected noise disturbances.
    
2.  Sound reflections can occur due to the presence of hard, level surfaces, resulting in reverberation or echoes in your recordings. This can give your tracks a hollow or distant quality, detracting from the desired intimacy and clarity.
    
3.  Try clapping your hands sharply in the room and listen carefully. If you perceive a fluttering sound or a prolonged echo, it indicates the presence of reverb issues.
    
4.  To address this, incorporate soft materials that can absorb sound. Consider using carpets, rugs, or thick curtains to significantly reduce reflections. Covering hard floors and, if possible, hanging curtains over windows, as well as placing furniture with fabric coverings in the room, can be beneficial.
    
5.  Avoid using hard surfaces as they contribute to the problem. If you cannot afford professional acoustic panels, you can utilize everyday items such as canvas paintings, tapestries, or foam tiles to break up these surfaces.
    
6.  When setting up your microphone, be mindful of its placement. Avoid positioning it too close to walls or in corners. Instead, aim for the center of the room or experiment with different locations to find the optimal spot with minimal reverb.
    

**Headphone bleed**

During recordings, particularly when capturing vocals, it is common for the audio from headphones to bleed into the microphone. This issue arises when the volume of the headphones is set too high or when open-back headphones are being used. This might be acceptable when recording for a song, but try to avoid this bleeding when recording for your voice model.

**Microphone placement**

For regular volume, it is recommended to position yourself about 2 inches away from the microphone. However, for louder phrases or when belting, it is advisable to increase the distance to around 4-6 inches. It is important to note that you should always stay closer than 12 inches from the microphone to maintain optimal audio capture.

> Creating Space for Belting
> 
> When engaging in belting techniques, it's important to allow yourself ample space, both in terms of microphone distance and the size of the room you're in. Excessive sound isolation, such as being confined in a closet or booth, or surrounding your microphone with foam, can easily result in overloading the microphone capsule. If you're unsure, it's advisable to incorporate more room sound when performing belted phrases.

Singing Languages[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#singing-languages)

**Basic custom slot**

Only one singing language will be supported in your voice model trained under basic custom slot.

**Pro custom slot**

Your voice trained under pro custom slot can go multilingual.

**Languages in your samples**

During the training process, each sample file will be processed individually and treated as a single-language file. It is important to avoid mixing phrases from different languages within the same sample file.

When uploading samples, please ensure that you place them under the appropriate language tab. Even if you are uploading samples for a basic custom slot, you have the flexibility to upload samples in different languages if needed. Keeping the samples organized by language will help maintain clarity and improve the training process.

**Upcoming languages**

We are continuously working on developing new singing languages for the custom voice feature.

For your new voice:

*   New languages will be supported by new pro custom slots.
    
*   New languages will be one of the options to be supported by new basic custom slots.
    

For your existing voice:

*   New languages will be supported when retraining your pro custom slots.
    
*   New languages will be optional when retraining your basic custom slots.
    

Singing or Speech[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#singing-or-speech)

Singing samples and speech samples can both be accepted for training your singing voice model.

Your voice can learn:

*   Timbre from your singing samples and speech samples, but plase note: for a person, timbre of speaking can be different to singing, which usually can not represent the true performance of singing.
    
*   Singing style from your singing samples
    

Your voice can't learn:

*   Singing style from your speech samples
    

File Quality Settings[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#file-quality-settings)

The audio quality of your samples directly impacts the quality of your voice.

We recommend you to set your audio quality in:

*   Bit Depth = 16-bit
    
*   Sample Rate = 44.1khz or 48khz
    
*   Lossless file format (.wav or .flac)
    

Post-Processing[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#post-processing)

To maintain the natural character and clarity of your target voice:

*   **No overlaps:** multi-layered vocals can complicate AI's analysis. Place the overlapped takes at back and stick to a single vocal track to ensure the AI can accurately process and learn from your samples.
    
*   **No hard cuts:** hard cuts can create abrupt starts or ends, which are not normal in a natural singing sound and can introduce clicks or pops. Use smooth fades at the beginning and end of the vocal clip for a more natural transition.
    
*   **No duplicating sections:** Duplicated sections don't help for the training. Your voice model benefits from the natural variation of performance.
    
*   **Control the volume:** Make sure your samples stay around 30-50% of your meter. Use a volume rider or automation to make sure volume levels are consistent across your entire dataset. The aim is to create a consistent volume level across the recording while keeping the dynamics within sections.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#training-your-voice)

Training Your Voice

After preparing your datasets, you can go to [Custom Voice Page](https://acestudio.ai/app/custom-voice/vocal-synth)
 to select a Custom Slot, upload your vocal samples, and start the training.

A Basic Custom Slots brings you a monolingual voice with 5 versions.

A Pro Custom Slot brings you a multilingual voice with 5 versions.

Click on a slot to start uploading your samples.

After all samples being uploaded, the training will start automatically. You can check the status by refreshing the webpage.

When you see the training page turns into the voice cloning management page, your voice is all set up. It will be shown in your voice library in ACE Studio. If you cannot see it, try to relaunch ACE Studio.

**Pro Tips**

If you are seeking exclusive performance and character for a voice, like the best results in different vocal ranges or emotions. It would be better to divide samples for several voices.

Here is an example:

Mike is a professional singer and would like to customize his own voice. He can both do well as tenor and bass. So it would be better to train 2 voice voices:

*   Train a high-tone&powerful voice based on samples that are mostly high-tone and powerful performances.
    
*   Train a bass voice based on samples that are mostly low-tone phrases.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#re-training-your-voice)

Re-training Your Voice

Click on the Retrain button to retrain your voice.

Retraining will remove your previous voice under this slot and take down any deployed singers associated with the voice. AI will start training a completely new voice from scratch using the new dataset. Prior to initiating the retraining process, you have the option to either retain the historical samples within this slot and upload additional new samples, or you can choose to clear the historical samples and only use the newly uploaded samples.

When preparing new samples, please note:

*   If the duration of newly added samples is significantly smaller than the already uploaded samples, for example, adding 1 min of new sample to a dataset of 30 mins, retraining may not bring about significant changes in the performance of the voice.
    
*   Retraining will not change the type of your slot.
    
*   You can switch the supported language of your basic custom slot by retraining.
    

**When should I retrain my voice?**

*   When your datasets has better quality or larger amount, you can use them to iteratively improve your voice
    
*   When you are not satisfied with the current result and want to adjust your datasets
    
*   When a new singing language skill being released
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#managing-your-voice)

Managing Your Voice

Versions[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#versions)

AI learns incrementally from your data, analyzing each sample in a step-by-step process. As learning deepens, the number of steps increases. Training with a small or limited-quality dataset, such as one not designed for singing but for speech, may require only a few steps. In contrast, a larger and more diverse dataset might necessitate additional steps for a thorough fit. However, excessive training steps can lead to overfitting, potentially degrading the performance of your voice with unpredictable outcomes.

By the end of training, you will get several versions based on different training steps from Rare to Well-done. You can find the best version by switching deployment and comparing each other.

Blend Voices[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#blend-voices)

Blending voices results in a hybrid voice. You can customize your voice to sound more like your target voice by adjusting the ratios of the blended voices. To do this, navigate to the slots management page and click the ‘blend voices’ button located under each version.

After blending, your voice will adopt the new voice characteristics. To apply these changes, you will need to refresh your voice by restarting ACE Studio.

Deploy to ACE Studio[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth#deploy-to-ace-studio)

For Basic custom slots and Pro custom slots, after deploying a version, you can switch deployment from one version to another. You need to re-launch ACE Studio after each deployment to refresh your voice library.

[PreviousDoubles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/doubles)
[NextPrivate Share](https://docs.acestudio.ai/voice-cloning/cloning-a-voice-for-vocal-synth/private-share)

Last updated 16 days ago

# Clip Editor | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

Double-click a clip to open the Clip Editor.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips/clip-editor#piano-roll)

Piano Roll


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![ACE Studio's piano roll.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fb2rs4Gbl9sUYnGoCyS0A%252Fpiano_roll.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf1523f2-ca9e-49cb-8cf9-19c1950428c2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4203e276&sv=2)

When the marker line is positioned on a MIDI Clip, the Clip Editor will display the Piano Roll for that Clip.

For Piano Roll editing of **Vocal Clips**, please refer to [Editing Notes](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/editing-notes)
.

For Piano Roll editing of **Instrument Clips**, please refer to [Editing Notes](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/editing-notes)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips/clip-editor#audio-editor)

Audio Editor


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F60gaYaFBOXW67LK9iQL2%252Faudio_viewer.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3fef63b-0ea0-4e28-aaa1-5455bc73ff57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17ab3a6&sv=2)

When the marker line is positioned on a Audio Clip, the Clip Editor will display the Audio Editor for that Clip.

*   Gain - drag to adjust the gain volume.
    
*   Stem splitter - click to open the stem split tool, where you can split the current audio being showed in this audio viewer into stems. This is the same tool as the [Stem Splitter](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/stem-splitter)
    .
    
*   Tempo analyzer - click to analyze the tempo of this audio.
    
*   Vocal to MIDI & lyrics convertor - click to open the vocal to MIDI tool, where you can convert this audio into a midi clip with lyrics on notes. For more information, please refer to [Vocal to MIDI & Lyrics](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-tools/vocal-to-midi-and-lyrics)
    .
    

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips/clip-editor#zoom-and-move-view)

Zoom and move view

![Zoom and move view in ACE Studio's audio viewer.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FceHjAYpxTYIbzH7vXiYb%252Faudio_editor_zoom.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d24ef5b-a3bf-4c5d-ad3a-61198edfefb2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3001764a&sv=2)

*   Drag horizontally on the time ruler to pan view.
    
*   Drag vertically on the time ruler to zoom horizontally. You can also hold Ctrl/⌘Command and scroll mouse wheel to zoom.
    
*   Drag with the middle button of your mouse on the grid to move view.
    

[PreviousClips](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips)
[NextRecord](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record)

Last updated 2 months ago

# 表现控制 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/biao-xian-kong-zhi#shen-me-shi-biao-da-kong-zhi)

什么是表达控制


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

表达控制是可以随时间自动化的参数，用于增加细腻度和真实感，允许你“绘制”效果应该生效的区域。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/biao-xian-kong-zhi#ke-yong-kong-zhi)

可用控制

颤音[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/biao-xian-kong-zhi#chan-yin)

颤音是音高的微妙且快速的波动，为声音增添温暖、表现力和丰富感。

分裂音[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/biao-xian-kong-zhi#fen-lie-yin)

分裂音是一种高级技术，通过同时产生多个音高来创建粗糙、有质感的声音。非常适合为旋律添加生硬、锋利的特性或紧张感。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/biao-xian-kong-zhi#bian-ji-biao-da-kong-zhi)

编辑表达控制


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FgxWb4Y6YdAaRYsH2Q7tl%252Fexpression_control.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0769fdd-d9c0-4ef9-8298-45c7bda1120e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=47877e4d&sv=2)

1.  在钢琴卷帘窗下方选择表达控制。
    
2.  单击并拖动以“绘制”要激活的区域。
    
3.  只需在活动区域上右键单击并拖动即可擦除。
    

[上一页演奏法](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/yan-zou-fa)
[下一页合奏](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou)

最后更新于1个月前

# Preferences | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

For windows users, you can find preferences under \[File\] form main menu.

For Mac users, you can find preferences under \[ACE Studio\] from main menu.

You can also click the gear icon in the lower right corner to open preferences.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#general)

General


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#language)

Language

*   **Interface**: Sets the display language for the entire user interface, including menus, buttons, and tooltips. By default, the application attempts to match your operating system's language.
    
*   **Default singing language**: Determines the default language assigned to any new singer track you create. The "In Singer's Native Language" option will automatically set the track's language to match the native language of the singer you select.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#auto-scroll)

Auto Scroll

These settings configure the automatic scrolling behavior of the timeline during playback, ensuring the playhead remains visible.

*   **Animation**: Customizes the style and speed of the auto-scroll animation when the view advances.
    
*   **Scroll Trigger**: Defines the point at which auto-scroll is activated.
    
*   **Scroll Dismiss**: Prevents auto-scrolling when you are zoomed in for detailed editing. For example, "<2.5s Scale" disables auto-scroll if the currently visible timeline represents less than 2.5 seconds, avoiding unwanted screen jumps.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#debug)

Debug

*   **Debug Logs**: Manages the storage of application log files, which can help developers diagnose issues. You can set how long logs are kept.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#midi-import)

MIDI Import

*   **Octave Offset**: Allows you to transpose all notes in an imported MIDI file up or down by one or more octaves.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#plugins)

Plugins

*   **ACE Bridge**: Here you can install or uninstall [ACE Bridge 2](https://docs.acestudio.ai/daw-integration/ace-bridge-2)
    . After the installation, if you find the plugin doesn’t work, you can also reinstall it here. ACE Studio will also notify you when a new version is available for update.
    

> This setting applies only to **macOS**. For **Windows**, ACE Bridge 2 will be installed with ACE Studio by the installer, and it can be reinstalled by the reinstallation of ACE Studio.

*   **Room Effect**: Here you can install [Room Effect](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/mixing/effects#room-effect)
    . This is a specialized audio effect used on Singer Tracks. If the effect is not working correctly or was not installed properly, you can use the Reinstall button to fix it.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#audio)

Audio


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For windows users:

Due to the exclusivity of ASIO, it can only support one program at a time. If you want to use an ASIO device, please make sure there is no other program using ASIO at the same time. For more informations, please refer to[ASIO Problem?](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#device)

Device

This section controls which hardware and drivers the application uses for audio.

*   **Device Type**: Selects the audio driver model for communication with your hardware.
    

> On **macOS**, this will typically be **CoreAudio**.
> 
> On **Windows**, it is highly recommended to select **ASIO** if you have an audio interface with dedicated ASIO drivers, as it provides the lowest latency and best performance.

*   **Input**: Choose the device you will use for recording audio.
    
*   **Output**: Choose the device for audio playback.
    
*   **Output Channels**: If your selected output device has multiple physical outputs, you can choose which pair to use here.
    
*   **New device Notice**: When this box is checked, the application will notify you if it detects that an audio device has been connected or disconnected, prompting you to review your settings.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#recording-and-playback)

Recording & Playback

These settings fine-tune audio performance, quality, and recording behavior.

*   **Sample Rate**: Determines the digital audio quality. Higher values like 48000 Hz or 96000 Hz offer higher fidelity but result in larger file sizes. 44100 Hz is the standard for CDs, while 48000 Hz is common for video and professional audio.
    
*   **Buffer Size**: Controls the amount of data processed at once, directly impacting latency.
    
    *   **Low Buffer Size** (e.g., 128, 256): Results in very low latency (delay), which is ideal for real-time recording and monitoring. However, it requires more CPU power and may cause clicks or pops on less powerful systems.
        
    *   **High Buffer Size** (e.g., 512, 1024): Increases latency but makes playback more stable and less demanding on the CPU. This is ideal for mixing and playback when you are not recording.
        
    
*   **Latency Compensation**: Manually corrects any timing discrepancies between your live input and the project's playback. If you find your recordings are slightly out of sync with the beat, adjust this value in milliseconds (ms) until the recorded audio is perfectly aligned.
    
*   **Pre-count**: Sets a metronome count-in before [recording](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/record)
     begins. Selecting "1 Bar," for example, will play one bar of metronome clicks, giving you time to prepare before the recording starts on the downbeat.
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#rendering)

Rendering


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Rendering** tab allows you to configure how the application generates the synthesized vocal audio. The application supports two primary rendering modes: the default **Cloud Rendering** and the performance-enhancing **Turbo Mode**.

These settings currently apply to vocal synth models Verse25 and later.

*   **Test Turbo Mode:** Click this button to start a 1-minute performance benchmark.
    
*   **Turbo Mode**: Once unlocked by a successful performance test, you can use this checkbox to enable or disable Turbo Mode.
    
*   **Pre-rendering:** When checked, the application will proactively start rendering vocals in the background immediately after you finish editing a note or parameter. This means the audio is often ready to play before you even press the spacebar, resulting in a more responsive and seamless editing experience.
    

For more information about rendering, please refer to [Local Rendering](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-rendering/local-rendering)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences#update)

Update


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can update to the latest version of ACE Studio manually here.

[PreviousACE Bridge 2](https://docs.acestudio.ai/daw-integration/ace-bridge-2)
[NextLicenses](https://docs.acestudio.ai/appendix/licenses)

Last updated 2 months ago

# 演唱合成模型 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku/yan-chang-he-cheng-mo-xing#mo-xing-shi-dai-yan-jin)

模型世代演进


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ACE Studio 持续迭代其人声合成模型。基于最先进的 AI 架构，我们融合专有创新以提升自然度、表现力、多语种准确性和声音克隆的保真度。

我们也在负责任地扩展人声音库，以覆盖更多语言和音乐风格。当架构改进和新训练数据达到我们的发布标准时，我们会发布新的模型世代。

# MIDI Tracks | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/midi-tracks#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

MIDI track can hold MIDI clips and host AI voice or AI instrument. You can create, insert, and record MIDI clips on a MIDI track and use the MIDI content to generate sounds with AI voices or AI instruments.

When AI Voice or AI Instrument is loaded onto an empty track, or when MIDI Clips are present on the track, it becomes a MIDI Track. According to the type of sound source attached, MIDI tracks can be divided into 3 sub-types: Non-source MIDI track, Vocal Tracks, and Instrument Tracks.

To create MIDI clips on a MIDI track, you can:

*   Double-click on the empty area of the track to quickly create a MIDI Clip;
    
*   Drag a MIDI file on the empty area of the track;
    
*   Record MIDI with a MIDI device, or sync MIDI from your DAW with ACE Bridge.
    

For more information about MIDI clips, please refer to [Clips](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/clips)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/midi-tracks#non-source-midi-track)

Non-source MIDI track


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you insert a MIDI clip on an empty track or unload the AI voice/AI instrument from a vocal/instrument track, it becomes a non-source MIDI track.

On this type of MIDI track, you can create and edit MIDI clips, but the track can only output sounds only with a standard piano sample library.

Click the + button on the track header or drag an AI voice or AI instrument onto the track header to turn it into a vocal track or instrument track.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/midi-tracks#vocal-tracks)

Vocal Tracks


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When AI Voice is loaded onto a track from the [Voice Library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library)
, the track becomes a Vocal Track.

*   You can drag and drop an AI Voice from the voice library on the track header.
    
*   Drop a new voice onto an existing vocal track header to replace the voice.
    
*   Turning on [Choir Mode](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)
     changes the Vocal Track into a Choir Track.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/midi-tracks#vocal-source-management)

Vocal source management

Click the image on the track header to open the track panel.

*   Track image: Click to open [Voice Library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library)
    .
    
*   Name: Double-click to rename.
    
*   Vocal Synth Model: Click to switch between different versions of the Vocal Synth Model. For more information about the Vocal Synth Model versions, please refer to [Vocal Synth Models](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/voice-library/vocal-synth-models)
    .
    
*   Language: Displays the languages supported by the current AI voice.
    
*   Settings:
    
    *   Copy and paste Vocal source.
        
    *   Change track image. The image for a Choir Track defaults to the loaded multiple AI Voices images and cannot be changed.
        
    *   Save your Choir/Blended as a preset, or save changes to the preset.
        
    *   Unload Model
        
    
*   Choir Mode: Click to enable Choir Mode. For more information, please refer to [AI Choir](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/ai-choir)
    .
    
*   Blend Voices: You can blend voices here. For more information, please refer to [Voice Blending](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-vocal-synth/creating-ai-vocals/voice-blending)
    .
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/midi-tracks#instrument-tracks)

Instrument Tracks


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When AI Instruments are loaded onto a track from the [Instrument Library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library)
, the track becomes a Instrument Track.

*   You can drag and drop an AI Instrument from the instrument library on the track header.
    
*   If you drop the instrument on an existing instrument track head, it will replace the instrument of this track.
    
*   Turning on [Ensembles](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles)
     changes the Instrument Track into a Ensemble Track.
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/midi-tracks#instrument-source-management)

Instrument source management

Click the icon on the track head to open the Instrument source management panel.

*   Track picture: Click to open [Instrument Library](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/instrument-library)
    .
    
*   Name: Double-click to rename.
    
*   Instrument Category: Displays the type of the current instrument.
    
*   Settings:
    
    *   Copy and paste Instrument source.
        
    *   Save your Ensemble as a preset, or save changes to the preset.
        
    *   Unload Model.
        
    
*   Ensemble: Click to enable [Ensemble](https://docs.acestudio.ai/ai-instruments/create-instrument-sounds/ensembles)
    .
    

[PreviousTracks](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks)
[NextAudio Tracks](https://docs.acestudio.ai/project/arrangement-in-canvas/tracks/audio-tracks)

Last updated 2 months ago

# 声音库 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

AI Voices 是 AI 歌声的声源。它们可以根据 MIDI 音符和歌词生成人声。您还可以通过编辑音符、歌词、音素、音高和演唱控制参数来进一步塑造演唱表现。

![The ACE Studio Voice Library window, showing a grid of available AI Voices.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FR8YDSdYs31ix0b3wYbEy%252Fvoice_library.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15a06c21-9af1-4350-aff7-255f992bb641&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a815c8a&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#fang-wen-ai-voices)

访问 AI Voices


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

有 3 种方式可以从声音库中浏览 AI Voices：

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#cong-gong-ju-lan-liu-lan)

从工具栏浏览

![Accessing the ACE Studio Voice Library by clicking from the main toolbar.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FuCnuPO6DxKowfK584hUh%252Fbrowse_voice_from_toolbar.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7eca0f19-19d4-4996-9829-5f236f53e12e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efa33fed&sv=2)

点击工具栏中的第一个图标以打开声音库，在那里您可以浏览所有可用的 AI Voices。将一个声音拖到画布上即可添加，或者点击一个声音然后点击画布以放置它。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#cong-hua-bu-liu-lan)

从画布浏览

![Opening the ACE Studio Voice Library by double-clicking an empty track on the canvas.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FmYCyS0gs3SyPZumLvb8y%252Fbrowse_voice_from_canvas.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df65e9032-8418-4248-8529-a5ac906dfb2e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5bbeed9&sv=2)

在画布上双击空的轨道区域以打开声音库，在那里您可以浏览所有可用的 AI Voices。然后选择一个声音进行添加。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#cong-ren-sheng-gui-dao-mian-ban-liu-lan)

从人声轨道面板浏览

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fiwrnptxi6HfFYC7VJHIj%252FClipboard-20251029-091531-781.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46d5044d-3581-4bd6-962e-172e76f8d7e3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=590f897d&sv=2)

点击人声轨道面板的图片以打开声音库，在那里您可以浏览所有可用的 AI Voices。您可以点击以替换当前的 AI 声音。您也可以点击 [AI Choir](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/chuang-jian-ai-ren-sheng/ai-he-chang)
 以访问声音库并点击将声音添加到合唱中。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#zai-hua-bu-shang-tian-jia-ai-voice)

在画布上添加 AI Voice

当您添加一个声音时，它会被加载到画布上选定或目标的轨道，并且在画布的相应位置会创建一个人声片段。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#sheng-yin-ku)

声音库


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

声音库中有 5 个选项卡，用于组织不同来源的声音：

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#yu-zhi-sheng-yin)

预制声音

预制声音由 ACE Studio 使用来源可靠的专业歌手数据集训练而成，高度呈现歌手的角色与演唱表现。我们会持续添加新的预制声音以满足多样的声音制作需求。

大多数预制声音为免版税，可用于任何商业作品。您可以在 ACE Studio 内轻松为免版税声音生成许可证。更多详情请参阅 [许可](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/fu-lu/xu-ke)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#ke-long-sheng-yin)

克隆声音

您克隆的声音会显示在此选项卡下。您可以从声音卡访问管理页面。想了解更多关于克隆您自己的声音的信息，请参阅 [为人声合成克隆声音](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-ren-sheng-he-cheng-ke-long-sheng-yin)
.

私下与您共享的克隆声音也会显示在此选项卡下。更多详情请参阅 [私密分享](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-ren-sheng-he-cheng-ke-long-sheng-yin/si-mi-fen-xiang)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#she-qu-sheng-yin)

社区声音

来自社区的声音会显示在此选项卡下。这些声音由 ACE Studio 用户社区克隆并发布。

要使用社区声音，您需要先 **收藏** 它，然后才能将其添加到您的项目中。

想了解更多关于发布克隆声音的内容，请参阅 [发布克隆声音](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-ren-sheng-he-cheng-ke-long-sheng-yin/fa-bu-ke-long-sheng-yin)
.

如果社区声音的所有者选择下架该声音，您在 30 天后将无法再访问该声音。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#hun-he-sheng-yin)

混合声音

您保存的混合声音会显示在此选项卡下。这些声音存储在您的账户下，登录您的 ACE Studio 账户即可在任何设备上访问它们。

右键点击声音卡以管理它。您可以修改其名称、标签、母语、图片，或从您的账户中删除它。

想了解更多关于混合声音功能的内容，请参阅 [声音混合](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/chuang-jian-ai-ren-sheng/sheng-yin-hun-he)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#he-chang)

合唱

预制合唱和您保存的合唱预设会显示在此选项卡下。

右键点击您保存的合唱卡以管理它。您可以修改其名称、标签、母语，或从您的账户中删除它。

想了解更多关于 AI Choir 功能的内容，请参阅 [AI合唱](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/chuang-jian-ai-ren-sheng/ai-he-chang)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#sou-suo-sheng-yin)

搜索声音

点击搜索栏以激活搜索模式。每个 AI 声音都有名称、母语和若干标签注释。您可以用文本搜索或使用筛选器定位所需的声音。

点击搜索栏右侧的关闭按钮以退出搜索模式。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku#an-sheng-yuan-he-cheng-mo-xing-shai-xuan)

按声源合成模型筛选

声源合成模型的筛选器位于声音库的右上角。您可以用它来筛选来自特定声源合成模型的 AI 声音。

同一 AI 声音可以被包含在多个世代的声源合成模型中，但由于不同模型之间的差异，该 AI 声音在不同模型中的表现可能有所不同。更多详情请参阅 [演唱合成模型](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku/yan-chang-he-cheng-mo-xing)
.

在默认的“所有模型”选项下，库中会显示所有 AI 声音及其推荐的声源合成模型。

[上一页路线图](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/lu-xian-tu)
[下一页演唱合成模型](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/sheng-yin-ku/yan-chang-he-cheng-mo-xing)

最后更新于14天前

---

# 发布克隆声音 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-ren-sheng-he-cheng-ke-long-sheng-yin/fa-bu-ke-long-sheng-yin#shen-me-shi-sheng-yin-fa-bu)

什么是声音发布？


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

如果你希望你的声音被全球制作人看到，可以将你的声音发布到创意库。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-ren-sheng-he-cheng-ke-long-sheng-yin/fa-bu-ke-long-sheng-yin#ru-he-fa-bu-wo-de-sheng-yin)

如何发布我的声音？


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

要发布你的声音，请点击你训练声音上的 分享 按钮。创建声音简介后，申请将发送到创意库团队。为保证创意库质量，团队会审查你的声音并决定是否通过。

请注意：发布到创意库的所有声音应为免版税。

[上一页私密分享](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-ren-sheng-he-cheng-ke-long-sheng-yin/si-mi-fen-xiang)
[下一页为声线转换克隆声音](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-sheng-xian-zhuan-huan-ke-long-sheng-yin)

最后更新于1个月前

# 效果 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

效果器面板用于为每个轨道添加和控制音频效果。

要打开效果器面板，请点击 FX 轨道页眉中的按钮或 [混音器](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/mixer)
 中想要编辑的轨道。

*   效果器面板将侧开并在您工作时保持打开。
    
*   效果器面板显示当前选定轨道的效果。
    
*   要关闭面板，请点击其右上角的收起按钮，或再次点击轨道上高亮的 FX 按钮。
    

![Open FX panel in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FCJLKJpIxUURBIfaibCiw%252Feffectpanel.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De346ba34-f510-4830-a783-2cbc27447921&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c200ae40&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo#ji-chu-xiao-guo)

基础效果


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

基础效果机架包含五个常用音频处理器链： **EQ3**, **EQV**, **压缩器**, **去齿音器**，和 **混响**。您可以使用“基础效果”标题旁的电源按钮开启或关闭整个机架。

![Basic Effects in ACE Studio.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FmJ4ekNzA59vULcRntKkA%252Feffect_pack.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a5269a3-c494-41e0-b971-1b47e8739df8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=947b87e4&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo#eq3)

EQ3

一个简单却有效的三段均衡器，用于常规音色塑造。

*   **低频**：调整低频的音量。
    
*   **中频**：调整中频范围的音量。
    
*   **高频**：调整高频的音量。
    

顺时针拖动每个旋钮可提升（增加音量），逆时针拖动可衰减（降低音量）相应频段。双击旋钮将其重置为 0 dB。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo#eqv-ren-sheng-jun-heng)

EQV **（人声均衡）**

一个基于预设的均衡器，针对人声进行了优化。选择四个预设中最适合您轨道在混音中角色的一个。

*   **主唱**：主唱的标准设置，带有轻微的低切和高频架增强，帮助主唱突出。
    
*   **明亮**：提供更强的高频提升和更高的低切，非常适合更明亮、更通透的人声音色。
    
*   **和声**：为和声或伴唱设计，降低低频和中频以避免与主唱发生冲突。
    
*   **合唱**：为合唱轨道量身定制，采用更宽的高通滤波以清理低频轰鸣并注重清晰度。
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo#ya-suo-qi)

压缩器

减少音频中最响与最弱部分的音量差，使声音更受控。

*   **阈值滑块**：拖动滑块以设置压缩器开始工作的电平。计量表实时显示音量被降低的程度。
    
*   **增益**：压缩后整体音量可能降低。使用此旋钮将信号提升回去。
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo#qu-chi-yin-qi)

去齿音器

抑制人声录音中刺耳的“s”、“sh”和“t”音（齿音）。

*   **阈值滑块**：设置去齿音器的灵敏度。降低阈值会减少更多齿音。
    
*   **频率**：使用此旋钮精确定位刺耳音的频率。常见范围在 4kHz 到 8kHz 之间。
    
*   **监听按钮**：点击此按钮可暂时仅监听去齿音器所影响的频率，这样更容易找到需要削减的频率。
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo#hun-xiang)

混响

为您的轨道添加声学空间感。

*   **预设选择器**：使用 < 和 \> 箭头在不同类型的混响空间之间循环。您可以选择 4 个混响预设：
    
    *   房间
        
    *   大厅
        
    *   教堂
        
    *   电影感
        
    
*   **干/湿**：控制原始未处理信号（“干”）与混响效果（“湿”）之间的平衡。在 0% 时不听到混响；在 100% 时只听到混响。设置为 10% 表示最终声音为 90% 干信号和 10% 湿信号。
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo#fang-jian-xiao-guo)

房间效果


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

注意：房间效果仅在歌手轨道上可用。

房间效果是一种特殊的混响，旨在模拟将虚拟歌手置于真实声学空间中，为合唱声音增加真实的深度与空间感。

此效果依赖第三方组件，首次激活合唱模式时系统会提示您安装该组件。

在房间效果的中心显示虚拟录音空间，每个带颜色的点代表合唱中的一位人声。

*   您可以通过拖动来排列人声位置。合唱与虚线之间的距离表示与麦克风的远近。
    
*   在右上角，您可以设置录音室的大小。
    
    *   8m X 8m - 录音室
        
    *   16m X 16m - 合唱大厅
        
    *   30m X 30m - 教堂
        
    

[上一页Mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/mixer)
[下一页文件管理](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li)

最后更新于1个月前

---

# 声线转换 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-gong-ju/sheng-xian-zhuan-huan#shen-me-shi-sheng-xian-zhuan-huan)

什么是声线转换


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

声线转换是一种工具，可将人声轨道中的声音转换为其他人声，甚至转换为乐器声音。声线转换不仅改变音色，还会调整某些风格元素，同时保持旋律和歌词不变。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-gong-ju/sheng-xian-zhuan-huan#ru-he-shi-yong-sheng-xian-zhuan-huan)

如何使用声线转换


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

声线转换作用于时间线上的选定区域。在画布上单击并拖拽以创建选区。这将定义要应用声线转换效果的精确区域。

有两种方式可以打开声线转换面板：

*   单击 **声线转换** 主工具栏中的 图标。
    

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fqdt51RKv0dPevUDanHAH%252Fvoicechanger_1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7df8ddd-a160-43db-9b35-4e84ae5eb0fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d93c809&sv=2)

*   在选中区域后，右键单击该区域以打开上下文菜单。导航到 AI 工具 子菜单并选择 **声线转换**.
    

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FPJB0NxUWIzH9iY250EuQ%252Fvoicechanger_2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a302cbe-6dd8-493b-9e28-ac76642459f4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f7a8036&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-gong-ju/sheng-xian-zhuan-huan#sheng-yin)

声音


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FGpIAtmVDNchvpI3KIcsv%252Fvoicechanger_3.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45931c73-e82d-45f7-a5d7-bacba5bcd404&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ec61d2b&sv=2)

声线转换面板列表分为三个选项卡：

*   **声音：** 包含所有预设的声线转换人声，这些人声可将源声音转换为目标演唱人声。
    
*   **乐器：** 包含所有预设的声线转换乐器，可将源声音转换为目标乐器音色。
    
*   **克隆：** 包含您所有自定义的声线转换人声和乐器。要了解有关为声线转换克隆您声音的更多信息，请参阅 [为声线转换克隆声音](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-sheng-xian-zhuan-huan-ke-long-sheng-yin)
    .
    

单击搜索栏以激活搜索模式。每个人声/乐器都有名称和若干标签注释。您可以通过文本搜索定位所需的人声/乐器。

要选择声线转换目标，请点击它。您可以一次选择多个要转换的人声和乐器。再次点击可取消选择。

点击人声或乐器的图片以预览其声音。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-gong-ju/sheng-xian-zhuan-huan#she-zhi)

设置


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FYP1iwwBDB4rPxcbpeLO6%252Fvoicechanger_4.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa305da7-192f-4ad8-a2a3-fec95b3a4078&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1683971f&sv=2)

选中人声/乐器后，您可以点击设置按钮来调整以下参数：

*   半音：以半音为单位调整音高。
    
*   音高校正：对音频执行音高校正。
    
*   按音阶校正：根据指定音阶执行音高校正。您可以选择音阶类型和模式。
    
*   随机偏移：以毫秒为单位添加随机时间偏移。
    

勾选 **去除伴奏** 在转换前去除源内容的伴奏部分。

勾选 **去除混响与和声** 在转换前从源内容中去除混响与和声。

点击 取消 以撤销当前设置更改并关闭面板。点击 **全部应用** 将设置应用到所有相关音频片段。点击 **应用** 将设置应用到当前选定的音频片段。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-gong-ju/sheng-xian-zhuan-huan#zhuan-huan)

转换


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FaMnOyvVYq3tcpHe0ORpq%252Fvoicechanger_5.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1ee992b-f652-4b9c-bc4c-fc0bbd469ad5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=378d3810&sv=2)

选定目标人声或乐器后，点击 转换 按钮开始转换。转换后的片段将出现在时间线下方。

如果您想转换为乐器音色，请注意以普通演唱人声作为输入源可能无法产生理想的乐器声音，因为两者在表现形式上存在显著差异。建议使用模仿乐器音色的人声音频以获得更好的转换效果。

要创建自定义的声线转换人声和乐器，请参阅 [为声线转换克隆声音](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/sheng-yin-ke-long/wei-sheng-xian-zhuan-huan-ke-long-sheng-yin)
.

[上一页本地渲染](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-xuan-ran/ben-di-xuan-ran)
[下一页音乐分离](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-gong-ju/yin-yue-fen-li)

最后更新于1个月前

# ACE Bridge 2 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

ACE Bridge 2 is a VST3/AU/AAX instrument plugin, as a bridge between your DAW and ACE Studio.

It can bridge audio from ACE Studio to a midi track in your DAW, and can also scan MIDI back to ACE Studio.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/daw-integration/ace-bridge-2#block-17508bffde80802b859ae6993bece7b7)

Installation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For Windows \- it will be installed with ACE Studio by the installer, and it can be reinstalled by the reinstallation of ACE Studio.

For macOS \- ACE Studio will ask you to install ACE Bridge 2 at the first launch. You can manage the installation from the preferences window of ACE Studio.

After installation, you should find it on the VST3/AU/AAX instrument plugin list in your DAW.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/daw-integration/ace-bridge-2#how-it-works)

How It Works


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FphelBShmpKYfYaSV7AB1%252FBridge_Light.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd78c6d79-fd03-4ce0-8419-5060235e8c0f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c2d0df8&sv=2)![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3596338706-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FkQIVmwbvhp2MPTfA3spu%252FBridge_Dark.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8cce355e-395d-4b6d-91fd-871a780d9e31&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=53e3f8ad&sv=2)

After inserting the plugin on a MIDI track in your DAW, you need to connect it to ACE Studio.

ACE Bridge 2 has three modes:

*   Piano Mode - The plugin will perform as a piano sampler, it will sound the MIDI notes on its track or any MIDI signals input from your MIDI device.
    

Please note: Under Piano Mode, ACE Studio will not sync the playback, and you will not hear sound output when you start the playback independently in ACE Studio.

*   Record Mode - The plugin will record all MIDI signals from the track during playback. When you stop the playback, it will send the recorded MIDI back to ACE Studio as a MIDI clip, and place them at the same place.
    
    *   The plugin will sync the playback to ACE Studio, but it is only one-way sync, when you start playback in ACE Studio, your DAW will not follow.
        
    *   You can set up which track to receive MIDI content from DAW.
        
    *   Polyphonic - Check this box if you want to input polyphonic, otherwise, the MIDI content will turn into monophonic when being brought to ACE Studio.
        
    

Please note: Under Record Mode, you will not hear sound output when you start the playback independently in ACE Studio.

*   Playback Mode - The plugin will bridge sound from ACE Studio to your DAW.
    
    *   The plugin will sync the playback to ACE Studio, but it is only one-way sync, when you start playback in ACE Studio, your DAW will not follow.
        
    *   You can set up which track to be bridged to DAW.
        
    

Each time you start playback, the plugin will update the current tempo and time signature to ACE Studio.

We will keep updating the bridge plugin with new features.

We'd love to hear your feedback: [\[email protected\]](https://docs.acestudio.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

If you can’t find the plugin in your DAW, please refer to [Can’t find ACE Bridge plugin in your DAW?](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/cant-find-ace-bridge-plugin-in-your-daw)
.

For Logic, Studio one, Cubase, and Reaper users, please check this [ACE Bridge 2: Special settings in DAW](https://docs.acestudio.ai/trouble-shooting/ace-bridge-issues/ace-bridge-2-special-settings-in-daw)
 while using the ACE Bridge 2.

**Debug Mode**

If you encounter any issues while using ACE Bridge 2, you can click the "?" button in the lower-left corner of ACE Bridge 2 to open the help panel, and activate Debug Mode in the upper-right corner to enable temporary log recording. The log files exported from ACE Studio will include the logs from ACE Bridge 2. Please send the log files to [\[email protected\]](https://docs.acestudio.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a9dadcd9d9c6dbdde9c8caccdadddccdc0c687c8c0)
 along with a description of your issue, and we will assist you in resolving it.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/daw-integration/ace-bridge-2#ace-bridge-1)

ACE Bridge 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Since version 1.9.7 of ACE Studio, ACE Bridge 1 is no longer supported. Please switch to ACE Bridge 2. If you still need to use the old bridge plugin, you will need to downgrade ACE Studio to a version earlier than 1.9.7.

[PreviousSong Templates](https://docs.acestudio.ai/creative-library/song-templates)
[NextPreferences](https://docs.acestudio.ai/account-and-settings/preferences)

Last updated 1 month ago

---

# 合奏 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou#shen-me-shi-he-zou)

什么是合奏


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

合奏是一个功能，允许您将多个 AI 乐器合并到同一轨道中，并将它们组织成一个统一的乐器组合。

您可以将自定义的合奏预设手动保存到乐器库中，系统也提供了若干预设可供使用。

要使用合奏预设，只需将其拖到画布上或拖到轨道头上。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou#shi-yong-he-zou)

使用合奏


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FYFEGK2AeF5nxv2rvywPO%252Fturn_on_ensemble.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D859c30a6-074f-4fb0-b124-f2a4d7bef16d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b9c8c59a&sv=2)

要使用合奏，请在 打开合奏 按钮来启用乐器轨道面板中的合奏模式。禁用合奏模式将清除所有合奏设置。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou#tian-jia-yi-chu-yue-qi)

添加/移除乐器

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F8alsfO0zcJhaT7VtxhxI%252FClipboard-20251029-102746-306.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1089729e-45bd-4ac1-8df8-cc0970ed6bdf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8313712c&sv=2)

*   点击 \+ 添加 按钮以复制现有乐器。
    
*   从库中将新乐器拖入以将其添加到合奏中。
    
*   通过拖动来排列乐器的顺序。
    

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou#can-shu-bian-ji)

参数编辑

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FCFFWYQDg9WzvHR2aKvtX%252Fedit_ensemble_parameters.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D660028ea-549e-4ed2-a428-22133f8c0683&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c428586&sv=2)

*   扩散（Spread）：控制合奏声场的宽度。
    
*   偏移（Offset）：调整乐器之间的微小时差以获得更自然的效果。
    
*   增益（Gain）：设置单个乐器的音量。
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou#he-zou-xiao-guo)

合奏效果


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

如果想营造空间感，我们建议启用房间（Room）效果。

要了解有关效果的更多信息，请参考 [效果](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou#ling-cun-wei-yu-she)

另存为预设


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FvASqpOiuyieB5t8jj7GY%252Fsave_ensemble_preset.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8409359c-5756-4d5b-940e-9cf94f03f920&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d4fcf4c&sv=2)

在轨道面板菜单中，您可以将当前合奏保存为预设。您可以自定义预设的名称和标签以便于检索。您保存的合奏预设将存放在乐器库的合奏选项卡中。

您保存的预设会存储在云端并与您的账户关联。

[上一页表现控制](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/biao-xian-kong-zhi)
[下一页走带](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai)

最后更新于14天前

# 乐器库 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FteV0fcDiEwBOePqpJbyZ%252Finstrument%2520lib.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd82fe4e9-c2a4-4e6e-a84e-9a74f554a217&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8edcaa42&sv=2)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#fang-wen-ai-yue-qi)

访问 AI 乐器


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

从乐器库浏览 AI 乐器有 3 种方式：

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#cong-gong-ju-lan-liu-lan)

从工具栏浏览

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FwwsVK2eB7QPmlfpLcXlj%252FClipboard-20251029-092355-375.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6933d79c-8018-4a79-889d-64b63b4a89b3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=29baa1a1&sv=2)

点击工具栏上的第二个图标以打开乐器库，在那里你可以浏览所有可用的 AI 乐器。将乐器拖到画布上以添加到当前项目，也可以先点击乐器再在画布上点击以添加。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#cong-hua-bu-liu-lan)

从画布浏览

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F7MgBwZI6HfJBf3visqMR%252FClipboard-20251029-092727-036.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b2bac1c-4ff7-490f-9ce4-181cfb7f85e7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77b3c78e&sv=2)

在画布上双击任何空轨以打开乐器库，在那里你可以浏览所有可用的 AI 乐器。然后选择一个乐器将其添加到当前项目中。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#cong-yue-qi-gui-dao-mian-ban-liu-lan)

从乐器轨道面板浏览

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FPOpklCFexydJDjVurlJ9%252FClipboard-20251029-092917-289.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72782a9b-c92b-4391-9a30-a7b47effd5ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=15a5755d&sv=2)

点击乐器轨道面板的图像以打开乐器库，在那里你可以浏览所有可用的 AI 乐器。你可以将乐器拖放到 [合奏](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#ensembles)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#zai-hua-bu-shang-tian-jia-ai-yue-qi)

在画布上添加 AI 乐器

通过上述操作，画布上对应的轨道将加载该乐器，并在画布的相应位置创建一个乐器片段。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#yue-qi-ku)

乐器库


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

乐器库中有 2 个标签：

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#yu-zhi-yue-qi)

预制乐器

预制乐器由 ACE Studio 使用专业音乐家及其演奏数据集以负责任的方式制作。这些乐器忠实地捕捉了原始演奏者的独特特性和表现力。我们会持续添加新的预制乐器以满足多样的音乐制作需求。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#he-zou)

合奏

预制合奏和你保存的合奏预设显示在此标签下。

右键单击你保存的合奏卡以进行管理。你可以修改其名称和标签，或将其从账号中删除。

要了解有关此功能的更多信息，请参阅 [合奏](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou)
.

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/yue-qi-ku#sou-suo-yue-qi)

搜索乐器

点击搜索栏以激活搜索模式。你可以通过文本搜索来定位所需的乐器。

点击搜索栏右侧的关闭按钮以停用搜索模式。

[上一页声音混合](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-ge-sheng-he-cheng/chuang-jian-ai-ren-sheng/sheng-yin-hun-he)
[下一页创建乐器音色](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se)

最后更新于14天前

# 导出文件 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li/dao-chu-wen-jian#dao-chu-yin-pin-wen-jian)

导出音频文件


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

单击 导出 从走带的按钮打开音频导出窗口，你也可以在\[文件\]菜单中找到“导出音频”。

> **键盘快捷键：**
> 
> Mac： ⌘ Command + Shift + R
> 
> Windows： Ctrl + Shift + R

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FcUZ8fOiwYxF5c3Kxjew0%252Fexport.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De823e5cd-7ffc-49cc-970c-9210d9ae18a0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e376e67&sv=2)

你可以将选定轨道在指定时间范围内导出为指定格式的音频文件。

*   渲染轨道：
    
    *   母线 - 将主轨导出的音频作为一个音频文件。
        
    *   选定轨道 - 将选定轨道逐个导出为单独的文件。
        
    *   所有单独轨道 - 将所有未静音的轨道逐个导出为单独的文件。
        
    
*   不导出演唱效果：导出时关闭所有人声效果。
    
*   导出范围：
    
    *   整个项目 - 导出整个项目的范围，从起始处开始，结束于最后一个片段。
        
    *   循环 - 导出循环区域的范围。
        
    
*   声道：此设置决定导出文件中的音频声道数。
    
*   格式：此选项让你选择导出音频的文件类型。不同格式在质量和文件大小方面有不同特点。
    
*   采样率：采样率指每秒捕获的音频样本数量。更高的采样率可以捕捉更多细节和更宽的频率范围，从而获得更高保真度，但文件体积也会更大。
    
*   位深：位深决定音频的动态范围——即最安静与最响亮声音之间的差距。更高的位深提供更大的动态范围和更低的噪底。
    

针对常见的音乐制作场景：

*   最高质量（母带处理、归档、发行）：用于最终母带或归档项目时，需要尽可能高的质量。
    
    推荐：.WAV，44100 Hz/48000 Hz，24 位。
    
*   个人试听与分享：在日常使用且需考虑文件体积时，MP3 是常用标准。
    
    推荐：.MP3，320 kbps。
    

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li/dao-chu-wen-jian#dao-chu-midiufdata-wen-jian)

导出 MIDI/Ufdata 文件


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FxpDjhpuFwO8uV5o6O6te%252Fexport_midi.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D648825cf-925a-41a4-ac1e-08b6a3e828e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=abb90a59&sv=2)

你可以在文件菜单中选择“导出 MIDI”来调出导出设置窗口，并将选区导出为 \*.mid 或 \*.ufdata 文件。

> **键盘快捷键：**
> 
> Mac： ⌘ Command + Shift + E
> 
> Windows： Ctrl + Shift + E

除了导出音符外，你还可以在导出设置窗口决定是否包含歌词和音素。你也可以选择将多轨内容合并为一个文件，或逐条导出每个 MIDI 轨道。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li/dao-chu-wen-jian#dao-chu-nei-bu-ge-shi-wen-jian)

导出内部格式文件


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li/dao-chu-wen-jian#cai-yang-.clips)

采样（.clips）

“\*.clips”是 ACE Studio 中采样的格式 [创意 库](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/chuang-yi-ku/cai-yang)
。它包含轨道和片段。

要导出采样，先创建选区，然后在文件菜单中选择“将选区导出为人声采样”。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li/dao-chu-wen-jian#mu-ban-.acet)

模板（.acet）

“\*.acet”是 ACE Studio 中模板的格式 [创意 库](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/chuang-yi-ku/cai-yang)
。它将整个 ACE Studio 项目文件夹打包为一个包。

要导出模板，请先保存项目，然后在文件菜单中选择“将项目导出为歌曲模板”。

[上一页导入文件](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li/dao-ru-wen-jian)
[下一页共享项目](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li/gong-xiang-xiang-mu)

最后更新于2个月前

---

# 在画布中编排 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

该 **画布** 画布是 ACE Studio 中的编排区域。在这里，您可以以片段的形式沿时间线创建、放置、移动和编辑所有内容来创作音乐作品。

在画布中，每一行代表一条轨道，片段可以放置在网格区域。画布的交互方式基于选区，而不是对象选中。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai/hua-bu)

# 界面导览 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/jie-mian-dao-lan#biao-ti-lan-he-zou-dai)

标题栏和走带


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FAt3WfZ5Cb0veTGkR7X5F%252FTitleBar%2520nd%2520Transport.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D998aef1c-f96b-4913-bdeb-b390d06a9339&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57bef487&sv=2)

标题栏和走带位于 ACE Studio 顶部，显示项目名称、速度、拍号和播放控制等核心功能。

[走带](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/jie-mian-dao-lan#hua-bu)

画布


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FSoVcQDfUm40IKsYUV9ZK%252FCanvas.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7bfdfc3f-8234-4fc0-b5c5-9f59e72cf457&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b9782f8&sv=2)

画布是音乐创作的核心区域，以时间线格式显示项目中的所有轨道和片段。在这里，你可以创建、移动、修剪和排列不同的片段，以构建完整的歌曲结构。

[在画布中编排](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/jie-mian-dao-lan#pian-duan-bian-ji-qi)

片段编辑器


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F5PehvJ12IkpbM6i4bKzM%252FClip%2520Editor.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29669713-64cb-4a20-ac55-10f7feeb5b7f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ecaa44ed&sv=2)

片段编辑器是用于精细调整的区域。当你双击片段时，它会在下方展开。你可以在钢琴卷帘窗中编辑音符、歌词和演唱控制，或在音频编辑器中调整音频文件。

[片段编辑器](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai/pian-duan/pian-duan-bian-ji-qi)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/jie-mian-dao-lan#tiao-yin-tai)

调音台


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FsXlbI36W1pg8ZIA2TVQi%252FMixer.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb8c2b36-1cbc-4dd8-a020-b193d4755829&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b81e6ff9&sv=2)

在调音台中，通过调整每个轨道的推子和旋钮，你可以轻松平衡各部分之间的关系并塑造最终混音。

[Mixer](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/mixer)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/jie-mian-dao-lan#fu-jia-gui-dao)

附加轨道


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252Fh7NK77DUH4538VlShBlW%252FAdditional%2520Tracks.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c93b3e7-92b3-4d46-8c72-de78de65d6b1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=962ee330&sv=2)

附加轨道可以在画布上方展开，用于管理项目的全局信息和标记。包括拍号轨、速度轨和和弦轨，便于你编排复杂的节奏。

[节拍与拍号变更](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai/jie-pai-yu-pai-hao-bian-geng)
[和弦轨](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai/he-xian-gui)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/jie-mian-dao-lan#xiao-guo-qi-mian-ban)

效果器面板


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FC4Fgoa08dD9iwGr8WXiS%252FFX%2520panel.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48c811fe-93f8-495c-92a0-3eabb5679984&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d8df7eb7&sv=2)

效果器面板是为声音添加“调味”的地方。在这里，你可以为每个轨道加载并调整效果插件。通过使用混响、均衡、压缩或 AI合唱 房间效果等效果器，你可以改变并增强轨道的音色。

[效果](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/hun-yin/xiao-guo)

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ru-men-zhi-nan/jie-mian-dao-lan#zhu-cai-dan)

主菜单


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252F7h9SQu4upQ9t3x799iVt%252FPreferences.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1df00a0b-1a30-48ce-9ca5-913c9cc89c5b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36cbec6d&sv=2)

主菜单位于 ACE Studio 界面的左上角。在这里，你可以找到文件管理、编辑操作和设置选项等所有命令。

[文件管理](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li)

# 走带 | ACE Studio Docs

ACE Studio 2.0 is currently in beta testing, and some features may not be fully launched.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#su-du-tempo)

速度 (Tempo)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Adjusting tempo in ACE Studio transport.](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FxYK5LUb3NFMVJYOFtWd4%252Ftempo.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6849240-5039-4b2f-8989-2531cb0eda2a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a88a53ba&sv=2)

拖动以根据当前时间线所在位置设置速度。（对于多速度项目，调整的速度仅应用于时间线所在的那一段。）

双击以输入精确的速度数值。

ACE Studio 支持 1-360 bpm 的速度范围。

如果您的项目包含速度变化，请参考 [节拍与拍号变更](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai/jie-pai-yu-pai-hao-bian-geng)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#pai-hao)

拍号


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FS1KiZlMLnET2Kthz0xC3%252Ftime_signature.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df42a234d-0ca8-4467-bfe5-71efec08bfb7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e719c5bc&sv=2)

拖动以根据当前时间线所在位置设置拍号。（对于多拍号项目，调整的拍号仅应用于时间线所在的那一段。）

双击以输入精确的拍号数值。

如果您的项目包含拍号变化，请参考 [节拍与拍号变更](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai/jie-pai-yu-pai-hao-bian-geng)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#bo-fang-lu-zhi-kong-zhi)

播放/录制 控制


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.acestudio.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1816898227-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fsn71WYzecYYQw3KkF40b%252Fuploads%252FLF6NFtUzCvu8lj8MZDap%252Fplayback_control.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D898a3c73-91ad-4362-94c7-0c30f29d6432&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=905f97ac&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#block-17208bffde8080b5a572c96b9713dbf1)

返回开头

点击将时间线跳回项目开头。

*   快捷键 回车
    

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#block-17208bffde8080939d09d25c8cdc0e62)

播放/停止

点击开始或停止播放。

*   快捷键 空格
    

播放始终从标记线处开始。如果您停止播放再重新播放，播放仍会从上次的起始位置开始，除非您移动标记线。

若要从停止处继续播放，请使用快捷键 Shift + 空格.

#### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#block-17208bffde8080bbb358d87884dca6ea)

录制

点击开始/结束录制。

*   快捷键 R
    

如果尚未开始播放，开始录制也会启动播放。您也可以在播放过程中开始录制。

有关录制的更多详细信息，请参考 [录音](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai/lu-yin)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#jie-pai-qi)

节拍器


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

点击开启/关闭节拍器。

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#xun-huan)

循环


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

点击切换循环模式开或关。

### 

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#xun-huan-qu-duan)

循环区段

启用循环模式时，时间标尺上会出现循环区段。您可以通过拖动其边缘来调整循环区段长度，或直接拖动来重新定位。也可以点击循环区段来开启/关闭循环模式。

选定区域后，使用快捷键 Ctrl/⌘Command+L 将所选区域转换为循环区段。再次按该快捷键可退出循环模式。

导出音频时，选择“导出范围为循环”可导出循环区段范围内的音频。更多细节请参考 [导出文件](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/wen-jian-guan-li/dao-chu-wen-jian)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#zi-dong-gun-dong)

自动滚动


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

点击此触发器以开启或关闭自动滚动。在播放期间，当时间线到达可见区域末端时，编排视图和片段视图会自动滚动。

在播放期间，如果您手动滚动视图，自动滚动将在下次播放前被暂时禁用。您可以点击以重新开启它。

您可以在首选项中设置滚动动画。更多详情请参考 [首选项](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/zhang-hu-yu-she-zhi/shou-xuan-xiang)
.

[](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zou-dai#shi-jian-ma)

时间码


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

显示时间线的位置。

[上一页合奏](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/ai-yue-qi/chuang-jian-yue-qi-yin-se/he-zou)
[下一页在画布中编排](https://docs.acestudio.ai/docs/product-wiki-zh/xiang-mu/zai-hua-bu-zhong-bian-pai)

最后更新于2个月前
